NA Shanghai , May 9 ( XINHUA ) --####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The spreading AIDS epidemic is threatening Asia 's economic growth , warned officials from the United Nations Program on HIV / AIDS ( UNAIDS ) , the World Health Organization and bank delegates at " Investing in Asia 's Health " , an Asian Development Bank ( ADB ) seminar held here Thursday .####[([1, 4], [12], [13, 50], 'Negative', 'Strong'), ([1, 10], [12], [13, 50], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA Statistics show that about two people in the Asia-Pacific region are infected every minute , and a total of over one million people were infected in 2001 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " AIDS is casting shadow on Asia 's economic miracle , and is turning into a global crisis , as the region accounts for 60 percent of world 's population , " says Michel Sidibe , Director of the Country and Regional Support Department of UNAIDS .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Research newly released by the WHO indicates that societies with a heavy burden of disease tend to experience a multiplicity of severe impediments to economic progress especially to sustainable economic growth .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It suggests that each 10 percent improvement in life expectancy at birth is associated with a rise in economic growth of at least 0.3 to 0.4 percent per year .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " With an alarming infection growth rate in many Asian Pacific countries , care for AIDS is over- burdening the health care system and is taking away from provision of other health services , " said Sidibe .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In countries such as China and India where AIDS was still at an early phase of the AIDS pandemic , timely control measures were critical to head off an explosive growth in infection , but these demanded heavy expenditure , he said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Jeffrey Sachs , director for the Center for International Development at Harvard University and chairman of the WHO Commission on Macroeconomics and Health , believes developing countries should fully recognize the importance of investing in health in their overall development strategy .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In his report , " Macroeconomics and Health : Investing in Health for Economic Development " , released by the WHO last December , Sachs estimated that total annual health outlays in world 's least - developed countries would rise by 17 billion U.S. dollars by 2007 and 29 billion U.S. dollars by 2015 and AIDS prevention and care would account for half the increase .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA However , low-income countries would be able to pay 14 billion U. S. dollars and 21 billion U.S. dollars respectively at best , said Sachs .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The WHO 's recommendations for each developing country include increasing investment in health and relevant areas like education , water and agricultural development ; the establishing of a temporary National Commission on Macroeconomics and Health ( NCMH ) , chaired jointly by the Ministers of Health and Finance to organize and lead the medical as well as economic war against AIDS and other diseases .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Sachs also addressed the exacerbating condition of the AIDS pandemic in China , saying that China had the technical ability to control AIDS infection , but still needed a comprehensive strategy , including local surveillance network , increasing government subsidiary and free medicine for the poor .####[([8, 12], [2, 3], [1], 'Neutral', 'Weak')]
NA The seminar is part of the serial activities of the ongoing 35th Annual Meeting of ADB 's Board of Governors .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Guantanamo to hold terror prisoners####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The U.S. naval base at Guantamano Bay , Cuba , once a detention center for thousands of Cubans and Haitians seeking freedom in America , may soon become a prison for men with a radically different view of the country .####[([39, 40], [35, 37], [32], 'Neutral', 'Strong'), ([22, 24], [21], [18, 20], 'Positive', 'Weak')]
NA The Pentagon is planning to house captured al Qaeda terrorists and Taliban fighters for an undetermined time at the base on the island 's isolated eastern coast , Defense Secretary Donald Rumsfeld said Thursday .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Despite the logistical hurdle of moving at least several dozen presumably dangerous men around 8,000 miles from Afghanistan , Rumsfeld called Cuba ` `the least worst place . ''####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA U.S. Rep. Ileana Ros-Lehtinen , R- Miami , said she supported the idea , in part , because it would underscore the naval base 's strategic importance at a time when some members of Congress have urged returning the territory to Cuba .####[([38, 42], [36, 37], [32, 35], 'Positive', 'Average'), ([12, 13], [11], [1, 4], 'Positive', 'Weak')]
NA ` ` It 's an excellent location , '' she said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ` ` It gives new life to Gitmo , '' as the base is often called .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Because the base is not on U.S. soil , people detained there are not entitled to American residency and eventual citizenship privileges .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA U.S. officials began using it as an offshore holding station during a Haitian refugee crisis in 1991 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA During the 1994 - 95 rafter crisis , 50,000 Cubans and Haitians were housed there in a tent encampment after U.S. naval vessels had picked them up at sea .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The prisoners from Afghanistan are not expected to arrive for weeks , and Rumsfeld said there are no plans to stage military tribunals or trials at the base , which is home to about 1,100 members of the Navy and Marine Corps .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The biggest challenge may be getting prisoners from South Asia to the Caribbean .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Some prisoners are reportedly being held on warships in the Afghan region .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Others are at a U.S. military compound in Kandahar , Afghanistan , where U.S. forces built a stockade of sorts to house them .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA 1999 PLANS####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA At the Southern Command in Miami , the Pentagon 's base for military operations in Latin America and the Caribbean , spokesman Steve Lucas said planners had pulled out blueprints from April 1999 -- when the Clinton administration had briefly considered housing up to 20,000 refugees from the Kosovo conflict at the base .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Britain's Prescott Pushes for Kyoto Pact Backing####[([5, 6], [3, 4], [1, 2], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA VANCOUVER , British Columbia --####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Kyoto Protocol on reducing greenhouse gas emissions must be ratified even without U.S. support , British Deputy Prime Minister John Prescott told an international conference on business and the environment on Friday .####[([1, 8], [15], [17, 22], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA Prescott said that while the U.S. decision to reject the Kyoto agreement is a cause for concern , pressure will be maintained on the Bush administration to go further with its current voluntary emission -reduction targets .####[([24, 36], [19, 22], [1], 'Neutral', 'Average'), ([10, 12], [7, 9], [1], 'Negative', 'Average')]
NA " This is the world 's best chance of dealing with a very serious threat to it , " Prescott told delegates from 65 nations at the Globe 2002 conference in Vancouver that ended on Friday .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Prescott , Britain 's front man in pushing the accord , said the United States until recently was critical of the science that led to the Kyoto pact but has now accepted it , and he remains optimistic that the goals of the United States and of other signatory nations would converge .####[([21, 28], [18, 20], [36], 'Negative', 'Average'), ([40, 52], [37, 38], [36], 'Positive', 'Average'), ([9, 10], [8], [36], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA The Kyoto Protocol calls on countries to reduce emissions of so-called greenhouse gases such as carbon dioxide , which are blamed by many scientists for global warming , to pre -1990 levels by 2012 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Named for the Japanese city where it was approved , the pact was signed by 84 countries , including the United States and Canada .####[([7], [8, 9], [0], 'Positive', 'Weak')]
NA Fifty - five countries responsible for 55 percent of emissions in 1990 must ratify it for it to take effect .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Forty - nine countries had done so as of mid-March , according to the United Nations .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Europe 's environment ministers have agreed that all 15 EU nations should adhere to the Kyoto Protocol .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Ratification could win support at an EU summit later this month in Barcelona , Spain .####[([1], [4], [0], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA The process is expected to be completed by June 1 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Prescott said the British program aims to cut emissions by 20 percent , and the country is now half way to that goal .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The issue has pitted business groups , who claim the accord will hurt the global economy , against environmentalists , who warn of the dire effects from global warming such as higher ocean levels and destruction of various plants and animal species .####[([28, 29], [22, 23], [19], 'Negative', 'Average'), ([10, 11], [9], [5, 6], 'Neutral', 'Weak')]
NA Canada is among the countries that have pledged to ratify the accord .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA The government is sharpening its newest weapon against white -collar defendants : the power to prevent them from paying their legal bills .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA And defense lawyers are warning that they wo n't stick around if they do n't get paid .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The issue has come to a boil in Newark , N.J. , where federal prosecutors have warned lawyers for Eddie Antar that if the founder and former chairman of Crazy Eddie Inc. is indicted , the government may move to seize the money that Mr. Antar is using to pay legal fees .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The warning by the U.S. attorney 's office follows two decisions by the U.S. Supreme Court last June .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In those cases , the high court ruled that federal law gives prosecutors broad authority to seize assets of people accused of racketeering and drug-related crimes , including fees paid to lawyers before an indictment .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If the government succeeds in seizing Mr. Antar 's assets , he could be left without top-flight legal representation , because his attorneys are likely to quit , according to individuals familiar with the case .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA A seizure also would make the case the largest -- and one of the first -- in which lawyers ' fees have been confiscated in a prosecution unrelated to drugs .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " The people who suffer in the short run are defendants , but the people who suffer in the long run are all of the people , because there wo n't be a vigorous private bar to defend the Bill of Rights , " says Gerald Lefcourt , a criminal defense attorney who says he has turned down a number of cases to avoid possible fee seizures .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA According to individuals familiar with Mr. Antar 's case , prosecutors issued their warning this week after one of Mr. Antar 's attorneys asked whether legal fees might be subject to seizure .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA TOKYO - Coral reefs will die from water that 's too hot .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Polar bears will have less room to roam , crowding some of them out of existence .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA According to a report released in 2000 by the National Air Issues Co-ordinating Committee on Climate Change , a group staffed by officials from the federal , provincial and territorial governments , hitting Canada 's Kyoto target may mean " the loss of roughly one year 's growth , or , viewed in absolute terms , in 2010 , the loss in annual economic output of approximately $ 40 - billion ( or $ 1,100 per capita ) . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA This is not a price worth paying .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Governments are expected to protect the national economy , and they should deviate from that mission only when crucial national interests are at stake ( fighting terrorism , for example ) .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Yet rising temperatures pose little threat to Canada .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In its authoritative Feb. , 2001 , report on the projected impacts of global warming , the Intergovernmental Panel on Climate Change identified several threats to Canadian ecosystems , but concluded that our farmers would generally benefit from warmer temperatures .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ( Non-farming Canadians , most of whom spend at least part of the winter months scraping ice off their cars , chopping firewood and shovelling their walks , will profit as well . )####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA As for the globally felt benefits that would follow from Canada 's implementation of the Kyoto protocol , they are slight .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA By 2010 , our $ 40 - billion sacrifice would yield an expected reduction in annual carbon and carbon - equivalent emissions of about 46 - million tonnes -- just 1/200th of the world 's total projected greenhouse gas output .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Even if Canada managed to convince the United States and every other Kyoto signatory to ratify the protocol , world carbon dioxide emissions would still soar .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA According to the U.S. Energy Information Administration , world energy consumption will increase by about 60 % between now and 2020 , with most of the upsurge expected to come from developing nations , which are not covered by the Kyoto Protocol .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Under the fully implemented treaty , carbon dioxide emissions would grow 26 % during the 1990 - 2010 period .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Without Kyoto , the figure would be 34 % .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The worldwide cost of that 8 % dip : about $ 2 - trillion in lost GDP -- give or take a trillion .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA There are better ways to spend that money .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Instead of trying to cap carbon dioxide emissions -- a costly burden at home and an impossible task in the developing world -- we should focus on abating the damage global warming does in at-risk nations .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If scientists are correct , higher temperatures and rising sea levels will depress grain yields in Africa and parts of Asia , fuel the spread of diseases , and threaten coastal nations such as Bangladesh and Senegal .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But these problems can be abated , or even eliminated , with Western assistance .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA While helping Third World nations plant new crops , vaccinate people and relocate coastal towns will be costly , the bottom line will likely be only a fraction of Kyoto 's 13 - digit price tag .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA A young Arab chemical engineer contacted him the next day , he said , to ask him to act as an intermediary in the sale of the nuclear fuel from the Kozlodui nuclear power plant .####[([17, 35], [15, 16], [1, 5], 'Positive', 'Weak')]

NA Researchers from the Weizmann Institute in Rehovot and the Technion in Haifa have developed a computer so tiny that a trillion of them could fit into a laboratory test tube .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The " computers " are biological molecules , using DNA for software and enzymes for hardware , and can solve a billion mathematical problems a second .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Such tiny devices could one day fit into cells and supervise biological processes , or even synthesize drugs .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA DNA strands exist in almost every body cell -- they are biological software that tell each cell and molecule what to do .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " If you look at the mechanism of a cell , a lot of what goes on inside is computation .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA We do n't need to teach the cell new tricks , we just need to put the existing tricks in the right order , " says Prof .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Ehud Shapiro of the Weizmann Institute , who headed the research .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Some scientists believe DNA - based computers could have an advantage over existing computers based on silicon chips .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Artificial chips have reached their limits and ca n't get any smaller .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But , say the scientists , tiny DNA strands can store huge amounts of information in minuscule space -- one cubic centimeter of DNA can store more information than a trillion CDs .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Prof .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Shapiro says the molecular computer is the first of its kind .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Although computers with DNA input and output have been made before , they have always involved a laborious series of reactions , each requiring human supervision .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " Previous biological computers were the same size as the room in which the supervisors and computer equipment worked , " said Shapiro .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " With the new method , all you need do to get an answer is put all the ingredients into a test tube , mix them together , and check to see what the output is . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA For now biological computers only know how to answer simple questions with a " yes " or " no " response .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA A typical question would be :####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In the sequence " AAB " is there an equal number of As and Bs ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Nevertheless , several researchers worldwide have hailed the computers as an important new development .####[([8, 9], [7], [3, 5], 'Positive', 'Strong')]
NA " They work better than anything I 've seen so far , " said Eric Baum , a computer scientist at the NEC Research Institute in Princeton , New Jersey .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Although he questions whether biomolecular computers will ever become really useful , he believes they are a " step in the right direction . "####[([15], [14], [13], 'Neutral', 'Average')]
NA Professor Shapiro and a growing number of other scientists believe DNA - based computers may lead to a number of useful applications -- they could be planted inside cells , where they would watch for irregularities or even synthesize drugs .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The computer simulates the cell 's natural mechanisms with an accuracy level of 99.8 percent .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Natural DNA processes also involve inaccuracies which are corrected by other genes , says Shapiro , and it is almost impossible to reach absolute accuracy using biological systems .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA However , for the uses for which the computers are designated , this level of accuracy is adequate .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA So how does such a computer work ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Let 's say the computer wants to know whether the number of times a " B " DNA type appears in a DNA section is odd or even .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The DNA section -- the " input " -- is inserted into a chemical solution along with enzymes to be used as the computer 's " hardware " .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Other DNA sections are added , which act as " software " .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA A software section sticks to the input with the help of an enzyme .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If the tip of the input is " B " , the input will be labeled as having an odd number of " B " sequences .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Another enzyme then cuts the section and reveals the next sequence .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Each time " B " appears , the label on the input changes from " even " to " odd " and back again .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Once the computer has dissected the entire input , it can determine whether the sequence appeared an even or odd number of times according to the last label -- the " output " .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The computer can also do other calculations , such as checking whether the " B " sequence appears at least once , or at most once , by inserting different types of software DNAs .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA On the contrary , the Kyoto Protocol requires most industrialised countries to achieve absolute emission reductions , while they still foresee to have growing economies .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Achieving this would only be a first step towards stabilising global greenhouse gas concentrations at a level that would prevent dangerous climate change .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA This is the ultimate objective of the Convention to which the US has subscribed .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA BUENOS AIRES -- Foreign multinational companies trying to avoid billions in losses furiously lobbied Argentine lawmakers and the new government ahead of today 's final vote on emergency legislation to devalue the peso and end the country 's decade- old currency parity with the U.S. dollar .####[([15, 46], [13, 14], [4, 6], 'Neutral', 'Strong'), ([0], [13, 14], [4, 6], 'Neutral', 'Strong')]

NA Argentina is now broke .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA GUANTANAMO BAY NAVAL BASE , Cuba --####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA You 're the first-ever American Muslim cleric to minister to a prison camp full of suspected terrorists and one confides he has a weapon .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Do you keep the secret ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Or do you breach religious confidentiality ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If you 're U.S. Navy Lt. Abuhena Mohammad Saiful -Islam you search for a third way to resolve the clear conflict of interest between the crescent moon pin stuck in your left lapel and the lieutenant 's bars on the right side of your uniform .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ` ` I will say , ` Give it to me , ' -- and not tell the general who had it , '' he says softly but firmly .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ` ` I 'll make sure that he does n't have it . ''####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA A 39 - year- old life-long , practicing Muslim , the soft-spoken Bangladesh immigrant is navigating uncharted waters and juggling complicated loyalties -- all while managing an international spotlight he has never experienced before .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA As a U.S. military chaplain , his contacts with prisoners are governed by the same confidentiality as that of a priest , minister or rabbi in the clergy corps .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Saiful -Islam is by training an imam , or a prayer leader , who guides the faithful in a mosque during the five-times - a- day Muslim prayer .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA At Camp X-ray , he is also serving the function of a muezzin , the person who announces the call to prayer , commonly from a tower called a minaret .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In his case , he is using a public address system and recording the prayer for five-times - a- day broadcast .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Sometimes he laughs uncomfortably when questioned by journalists .####[([5, 8], [3, 4], [2], 'Negative', 'Average')]
NA Sometimes he looks bewildered .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But mostly he 's a busy man , trying to soothe Muslim sensitivities over the rugged chain - linked - fence cells at Camp X-ray .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Advocate####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Saiful -Islam arrived at the detention center for suspected terrorists on Jan. 24 and made his debut by chanting the pre-dawn call to prayer to wake up alleged leaders of Afghanistan 's Taliban militia and members of Osama bin Laden 's al Qaeda network .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Since then , he has emerged as their advocate , arguing that the U.S. military can safeguard its soldiers while adding a few amenities of everyday Islamic life .####[([0], [9], [4], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA Soon , he says , traditional white knit skullcaps will arrive for the captives to top off their fluorescent orange jumpsuits .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Until he emerged as the chaplain of choice for this special assignment from among only 14 Muslim clerics in the U.S. armed forces , he was the only cleric specifically assigned to a Marine Corps base -- at Camp Pendleton , Calif .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA NEW DELHI , April 22 -- INTERNATIONAL call charges have finally started tumbling down , with Bharti Telesonic Ltd -- the long-distance arm of the Bharti group offering tariffs that are up to 40 percent lower than the existing rates .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Announcing this at a news conference , Mr Sunil Mittal , Chairman &amp ; amp ; Managing Director , Bharti Enterprises , noted that the tariffs , which would be made available on its ILD [ international long distance ] services being launched on May 1 , would be revised downwards as and when the market demanded it .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " The present rate cut of up to 40 percent on peak -time rates is likely to be lowered after Videsh Sanchar Nigam Ltd ( VSNL ) and the other ILD operators , who are yet to begin services , announce their rates .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Unlike the STD [ subscriber trunk dialing ] services where a further rate cut may not be feasible , in the international services there is scope for more improvement , " he said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA As per the tariff plan announced by Bharti , peak - time call charges to the SAARC [ South Asian Association for Regional Cooperation ] region will be offered at Rs 21.18 per minute as against the present Rs 21.82 , while for the rest of the world it will be Rs 24 per minute as against Rs 31.30 to Rs 40 that are applicable now .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA For non-peak hours , the call rates for the SAARC regions are being lowered to Rs 18 from Rs 18.95 per minute and for the rest of the world at Rs 21.18 per minute from the current Rs 27.69 to Rs 36 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Mr Mittal noted that although the original plan was to launch the ILD services ( IndiaOne ) by the middle of this month , the company was still awaiting security clearances and the commissioning certificate from the Department of Telecommunications ( DoT ) .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Interconnect agreements had already been signed with almost all cellular operators .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA They include AT&amp ; amp ;T , Sprint , Teleglobe , Eteselat , Saudi Telecom , British Telecom and SingTel to name a few .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA These nine carriers account for 90 percent of the traffic coming to India .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " Bharti , after requisite clearances , will offer its network to all carriers on a non-discriminatory basis .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Carriers will now connect to Bharti 's network and enjoy rates that will enable them to offer deep discounts to the end-consumer .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA A total investment of Rs 100 crore is planned for the project , of which Rs 75 crore has already been spent , " he said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA IndiaOne had laid approximately 14,000 km of optical fibre cable covering 90 cities .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The company has contracted submarine cable capacity from network i2i , and backed it up with satellite connectivity to build in redundancy .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The ILD network is based on IP [ Internet Protocol ] centric backbone .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The multiservices platform comprises TDM [ Time Division Multiplexing ] switch layer , an ATM [ Asynchronous Transfer Mode ] and IP layer and intelligent network to offer value-added services , he said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA The number of employees working on a temporary or daily basis have increased drastically as companies moved to slash labor costs after the financial crisis in 1997 , the National Statistical Office ( NSO ) said Friday .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA NSO statistics showed that the number of workers employed on a temporary and daily basis rose by 888,000 to 6,962,000 in October compared with late 1997 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The number working on a temporary basis went from 4,182,000 in late 1997 to 4,641,000 last month and that for those hired on a daily basis surged to 2,321,000 from 1,892,000 during the cited period .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The number of full-time workers declined 626,000 to 6,525,000 during the same time span .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " Demand for those working on a temporary or daily basis is risiing because companies are trying to save labor costs amid the continued economic slowdown , " an NSO official said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Over 90 percent of full-time workers receive retirement allowances and bonuses but the comparable numbers fell to 10 percent for temporary workers and 1 percent for those employed on a daily basis .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA About 80 to 90 percent of full-time workers were registered for the national pension , employment and health insurance systems while the comparable numbers shrank to 20 percent and 2 to 3 percent for temporary workers and those hired on a daily basis , respectively .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Amman -- Jordan , bound by environmental clauses in the Free Trade Agreement ( FTA ) with the US , is currently mulling over signing the Kyoto Protocol on global warming even though Washington turned down the protocol six months ago .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Having clauses on the protection of environmental and labour rights in the body of the FTA does not stop the government from signing environmental agreements refused by the US , according to Minister of Municipal and Rural Affairs and the Environment Abdul Razzaq Tbeishat .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA He explained to The Jordan Times that " in Jordan , we conclusively believe that development cannot be achieved unless the environment is protected . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Certain steps have to be taken with regard to this objective -- including signing the Kyoto deal , he said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA He announced the government 's intentions to sign the Kyoto treaty on Sunday during a workshop on climate change , organised by the ministry and the United Nations Development Programme ( UNDP ) .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In 1992 , Jordan signed the UN Climate Change Convention that compels nations to curb global warming , which is blamed on gases produced by factories and cars that burn fuel .####[([13, 17], [12], [6, 10], 'Neutral', 'Weak')]
NA The Kyoto climate treaty is another international effort to limit greenhouse gases and fight global warming .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Asked whether signing the Kyoto Protocol will affect Jordan and US efforts to upgrade the Kingdom 's environmental framework , Tbeishat said that signing the protocol will have a " positive " outcome on Jordan .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA He explained that both the US and Jordan have different issues to deal with on a national level , including environmental issues .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " In the US , they have their own circumstances , " the minister said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " But here , we are a developing country and we care about having clean industry ... the whole world knows our position , [ which is ] to achieve sustainable development . "####[([14, 16], [12], [0], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA The Kyoto Protocol was agreed upon by 160 countries under the United Nations Framework Convention on Climate Change ( UNFCCC ) .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The convention was created in 1992 , and adopted in Kyoto , Japan , in 1997 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Under the agreement , industrialised nations must reduce their emissions of greenhouse gases by an average of 5.2 per cent ( from 1990 levels ) from between 2008 to 2012 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA After the Clinton administration signed the Kyoto Protocol in November 1998 , the new Bush administration overturned the decision last April , as the US was facing a faltering economy and rising energy prices .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Even More " Proving Rape "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Chatterbox feels that the Wall Street Journal editorial page 's coverage of Juanita Broaddrick 's rape charges against Bill Clinton ( see " Proving Rape , " " More Proving Rape , " as well as Michael Kinsley 's " Readme " column in the current issue ) cries out for the introduction of the Scientific Method into the usually mushy business of assessing press responsibility .####[([4, 20], [2], [1], 'Neutral', 'Average')]
NA With that in mind , Chatterbox hereby inaugurates the Intellectual Dishonesty ( henceforth to be known as the Indis ) Index .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Here 's how it works :####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Publications that refuse to acknowledge ( even if to refute the importance of ) highly significant but inconvenient facts in their news or opinion coverage of controversial events will score one point for the initial offense .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA They will then score one point for every subsequent issue or broadcast or Internet posting after the first offense is noted by Chatterbox if they continue not to report said inconvenient fact -- and an additional two points on days when the news organization runs a follow - up without making note of said inconvenient fact .####[([19], [21], [23], 'Negative', None)]
NA Publications receiving a score of 10 will be inducted into the Indis Hall of Fame .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Publications that get all the way up to 20 will be faxed a likeness of Joseph Stalin .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ( Chatterbox would prefer not to invoke the phrase " intellectual dishonesty , " because it 's pompous and falsely suggests that only intellectuals can be intellectually dishonest .####[([10, 14], [3, 14], [2], 'Neutral', 'Average')]
NA But Chatterbox does n't know any other easily understandable phrase that describes this particular kind of offense . )####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA For the purposes of this survey , the Wall Street Journal will be counted as a separate and distinct publication from the Journal 's editorial page , because , in essence , it is .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Journal editorial page continues not to acknowledge that Norma Kelsey , the friend and employee to Juanita Broaddrick who is one of two people partially corroborating Broaddrick 's rape accusation , is the daughter of a man whose murderer was pardoned by Gov. Bill Clinton .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ( A responsible account of the whole controversy in today 's New York Times reports that Kelsey says the pardon had nothing to do with her corroboration . )####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Journal editorial page gets one point for failing to note the pardon in its initial Op - Ed by Dorothy Rabinowitz on Feb. 19 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Because it has published three times since the initial omission , it scores an additional three points .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA And because it published an editorial Feb. 22 taunting the rest of the press for not following it on the story -- and still did n't mention the pardon -- it scores an extra two points .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA That comes to a total of six .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Chatterbox feels certain that the Journal editorial page will provide some follow - up tomorrow to tonight 's NBC broadcast of its own Broaddrick interview , which means that if the Journal editorial page continues to take no action it will be in the Indis Hall of Fame by Monday at the latest !####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Chatterbox considered but rejected the idea of awarding Rabinowitz bonus points for having " eventually convinced " Broaddrick to grant an interview to the New York Times ( as the Times reports in today 's story ) .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But the Scientific Method does not permit any tinkering with the Indis Index 's scoring procedures .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA And besides , Rabinowitz 's efforts on the Times ' behalf were n't really unethical , just puzzling , given the two newspapers ' intense rivalry .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA When Chatterbox asked the Journal 's DC bureau chief , Alan Murray , who exercised good judgment in not breaking the Broaddrick story ( and - - full disclosure -- is Chatterbox 's former boss ) , to comment about a Journal employee 's feeding sources to the Times , he replied : " I do n't really have any comment on what the edit page did .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA They do their thing , we do ours . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Which is what Journal news employees are instructed to say whenever the editorial page causes them cringing embarrassment .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA For her part , Rabinowitz explains to Chatterbox that her efforts on behalf of the Times were more indifferent than the Times made them sound .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " Ms. Broaddrick told me Sunday that a Times reporter had appeared at the house in the a.m. , and that she had refused an interview , " Rabinowitz writes in an e-mail message .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Dushanbe , 21 July : A patrol of Russia 's border guards discovered two sacks filled with narcotics on the Moskva border detachment 's section of the Tajik - Afghan border on Friday [ 20 July ] .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA An expert examination showed that the sacks contained 86.9 kilos of pure heroin , head of the press service of Russia 's Border Troops in Tajikistan Colonel Aleksandr Kondratyev told ITAR - TASS on Saturday .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Recent weeks have seen important developments on both sides of the Atlantic for the policy pursued in combating climate change .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In Europe , the council of environment ministers concluded a formal political agreement on 4 March on the decision to ratify the Kyoto Protocol before 1 June this year .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA With this major decision , the European Union is opening the door to the entry into force of the Kyoto Protocol for climate protection just in time for the world summit on sustainable development to be held in August 2002 in Johannesburg .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In the United States , on 14 February President Bush presented the US national climate protection program .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It should be remembered that after Bush described the Kyoto Protocol as " fundamentally flawed " international negotiations on climate protection almost collapsed .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The United States , the world 's biggest emitter of greenhouse gases ( 25 percent of global emissions ) withdrew from an international agreement that , for the first time , set binding targets for developed countries for climate protection .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA We now know that the US withdrawal did not stop the world community from deepening this important multilateral agreement for combating climate change .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The European Union played a dominant role in these negotiations and the community of states concluded , at the Bonn and Marrakech conferences of July and October last year , an agreement that sets out how to implement the Kyoto Protocol and provides for an original mechanism for respecting the reduction obligations that could possibly serve as a model for other agreements and that suggests a possible strengthening of international institutional structures in the environmental field .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA This must now be ratified by all the parties and will shortly enter into force .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA However , all the parties repeated with insistence that world climate protection cannot be effective unless the United States takes measures that are comparable to these taken by Europe and Japan .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Unfortunately , the recent US climate protection program falls far short of meeting such expectations .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Although there is a certain satisfaction at seeing President Bush recognize the need to fight climate change , that must not in any way conceal the extreme weakness of what he announced .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Under the US program , US emissions as a proportion of GDP must fall by 18 percent between 2002 and 2012 , or in other words energy efficiency must increase by 18 percent .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA This can hardly be described as ambitious as a 15 percent increase in energy efficiency was in any event expected given present productivity levels .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In addition , if the US economy continues to grow , the increased energy efficiency will be cancelled out or more than cancelled out .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA With an annual economic growth objective of 3 percent , absolute US emissions in 2012 will be 24.5 percent more than 1990 levels , despite the improvement in energy efficiency .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA By comparison , respect for the Kyoto Protocol requires the EU to reduce its emissions by 8 percent compared with 1990 , Japan by 6 percent , and the United States by 7 percent , a figure accepted by President Clinton in 1997 .####[([6, 8], [4], [0], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA The warnings by climate experts went unheeded in the US climate protection program .####[([0], [1, 2], [4, 5], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA In its last report , the IPCC [ Intergovernmental Panel on Climate Change ] called for rapid and decisive action to at least avert the most serious consequences of climate change .####[([17, 20], [15, 16], [6, 7], 'Positive', 'Weak')]
NA Scientists estimate that the industrialized countries must reduce their emissions to around 70 percent by 2020 to maintain climate change at an acceptable level .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Researchers have shown that without a determined policy on climate coordinated at international level the consequences of climate change will be dramatic .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The average global temperature will increase by 5.8d C by 2100 , sea levels will rise by up to 90 cm over the same period , and there will be an increasing number of hurricanes with ever more serious consequences , while man and nature will have to cope with a shift in climate and rainfall zones the like of which has never been seen before .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA At our instigation , on 4 March EU environment ministers therefore called on the United States to " assume its responsibilities under the framework agreement on climate change , " that is to stabilize greenhouse gas emissions at 1990 levels and strengthen domestic actions to bring them into line with the level of effort accepted by the industrial countries in application of the Kyoto Protocol .####[([14, 28], [12, 13], [8, 10], 'Neutral', 'Weak')]
NA If the effects of climate change were not so devastating and our action were to be guided by economic competition , we Europeans could welcome the fact that the United States is not committing itself to an ambitious climate protection program , in so far as the technologies in the field of energy efficiency and renewable energy are the technologies of the future .####[([26, 41], [24, 25], [22, 23], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA Anybody who fails to exploit these markets from the outset will remain lagging behind .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Demand for these technologies is increasing worldwide .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The " three liters for 100 kilometers " car , high efficiency turbines , and solar panels are export successes and their development is driven by a climate protection policy of growing amplitude .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Even today it is difficult to find buyers outside the United States for the fuel- guzzling cars of the US automobile industry .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA US reticence is not therefore a reason for us to reduce our climate protection efforts .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The dominant role of the European climate protection policy has benefits for our economy .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Many studies show that an active policy of climate protection is not in any way contrary to a policy of full employment .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA On the contrary , it can have a positive effect .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA US human rights report invites scorn####[([1, 4], [6, 5], [0], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA Author : CHIDANAND RAJGHATTA - TIMES NEWS NETWORK [ TUESDAY , MARCH 05 , 2002 1:21:47 PM ]####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA WASHINGTON : Unprecedented scepticism and scorn accompanied the release by the United States on Monday of its annual human rights report amid charges of hypocrisy and double standards arising from the ongoing war on terrorism .####[([17, 21], [4, 6], [0], 'Negative', 'Strong'), ([17, 21], [23, 24], [0], 'Negative', 'Weak')]
NA Washington 's kid glove treatment of its so-called allies such as Saudi Arabia and Pakistan came up for withering scrutiny at a briefing to release the 2001 Country Reports on Human Rights Practices , an annual administrative exercise mandated by the Congress that many feel has increasingly become a meaningless ritual .####[([1, 15], [19, 20], [0], 'Negative', 'Strong'), ([35, 42], [45], [44], 'Negative', 'Weak')]
NA Amid widespread domestic criticism over curtailment of civil liberties , US officials laboured to convince a disbelieving press corps that the exercise was evenhanded .####[([6, 9], [2, 4], [3], 'Negative', 'Average')]

NA TAIPEI , Sept 27 ( AFP ) -- Taiwan is expected to officially become a full member of the World Trade Organization ( WTO ) in March 2002 , Vice Minister of Economic Affairs Steve Chen said Thursday .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " March appears to be a more reasonable estimate while earlier admission cannot be entirely ruled out , " according to Chen , also Taiwan 's chief WTO negotiator .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA After having secured the approval of a working panel in Geneva , Taiwan 's entry has yet to be ratified at the WTO 's ministerial meeting set for Qatar in November and then undergo parliamentary deliberation at home , he said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Chen said Taiwan is set to reduce the average tariff rate on 1,021 farm products to 12.9 percent after its WTO accession from 20.0 percent currently .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " We will also phase out internal protection of such products and remove export subsidies . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA At the same time , the average tariff rate on 3,470 industrial items would be slashed to 4.2 percent eventually from the current 6.0 percent , he added .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Under a quota system , the tariffs on imported cars would be reduced from 30.0 percent in the first year after Taiwan 's WTO entry to 17.5 percent in 10 years , he said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Chen said Taiwan 's external trade has less of a need to readjust itself in the post - WTO era as it has long functioned under a market -oriented economy and already largely conforms to international conventions .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Taiwan -made products stood a good chance of becoming even more competitive thanks to wider access to overseas markets and lower costs for material imports , he said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA However an expected increase in farm imports would certainly have an impact on the domestic agricultural sector , he said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The vice minister said Taiwan 's service industry was unlikely to sustain an excessive impact as it has been largely opened to private and foreign participation .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Instead , service ventures in the financial , transport and telecom sectors should benefit from the introduction of advanced skills and expertise from abroad , he added .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Africa Endorses Mugabe Victory , the West Condemns It####[([9, 8], [8], [7], 'Negative', 'Strong'), ([3, 4], [2], [1], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA Author : Ofeibea Quist-Arcton Credit : allAfrica.com Dateline : Harare####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA International reaction to the controversial re-election of Zimbabwean president Robert Mugabe to another six year term varied widely .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA African observers generally approved of his victory , while Western governments denounced it .####[([6, 7], [3, 5], [1, 2], 'Positive', 'Average'), ([13], [12], [10, 11], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA Observer missions from South Africa , Nigeria , Namibia and the Organisation of African Unity ( OAU ) respectively , described the poll as " legitimate " - largely satisfactory and transparent , credible , free and fair .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA All three observer teams noted long queues and delays in chaotic voting .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Namibians went as far as to say Zimbabwe 's election system was " water tight , without room for rigging " .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The South African observer team blamed the long lines of voters unable to vote despite waiting many hours on " administrative oversights " , a description that drew audible laughter from journalists and diplomats attending their press conference in the capital , Harare on Wednesday .####[([26], [29, 31], [32, 41], 'Negative', 'Average')]
NA President Daniel arap Moi of Kenya congratulated Mugabe , calling his victory " testimony of the confidence and high esteem the people of Zimbabwe hold in you . "####[([27], [25, 26], [1, 6], 'Neutral', 'Weak'), ([8], [7], [1, 6], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA The observations of the 14 - member Southern African Development Community ( SADC ) Parliamentary Forum team differed considerably from the other African missions .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In sharp contrast to other African observer teams , the forum said the conduct of the elections fell short of regional expectations .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " The climate of insecurity obtaining in Zimbabwe since the 2000 parliamentary elections was such that the electoral process could not be said to adequately comply with the norms and standards for elections in the SADC region , " the forum said in a statement .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA That position chimed closely with views expressed by the main Zimbabwean monitoring group , the Zimbabwe Election Support Network which had 400 observers monitoring the poll and have been heavily critical .####[([25, 26], [28, 31], [15, 19], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA The SADC parliamentarians ' view was also echoed by the Norwegian observer delegation which said , on Tuesday , that the election failed to meet international standards .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Norway Prime Minister Jan Petersen said in a statement that " The presidential election in Zimbabwe has not satisfied the fundamental requirements for a democratic election . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Mugabe 's main challenger , Morgan Tsvangirai of the Movement for Democratic Change , has rejected the outcome of the presidential poll .####[([17, 22], [15, 16], [1, 13], 'Negative', 'Average')]
NA He said the result was " illegitimate " and a clear case of " highway robbery " by Mugabe , his government and his party , Zanu - PF .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Tsvangirai warned that his disenfranchised supporters were " seething " but implored them to stay calm .####[([13, 16], [12], [1], 'Neutral', 'Strong'), ([0], [12], [1], 'Neutral', 'Strong'), ([4, 10], [2], [1], 'Negative', 'Average'), ([0], [7, 9], [1], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA The MDC leader said systematic cheating , spoiling tactics , rigid new laws and sheer obstruction - as well as political violence and intimidation - were just some of the irregularities practised by the authorities in the run-up to , and during the poll .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Mugabe was announced the winner with 56.1 percent of the vote , leaving Tsvangirai trailing behind with 42 percent .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
