NA Chapter 5 A Physics of Semantics ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ach of the chapters of Investigations broaches new territory .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Each is tentative and incomplete , pointing but not fully adequate .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Yet , I persistently hope , it is better to light one candle against . . . what ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA the darkness ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA the veil beyond which we have had no framework of questions before ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA There are grounds , reasoned about by the best of philosophers and scientists of the past several centuries , to doubt a physics of semantics .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA We are on shaky ground .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Yet when the first hard frost comes , when the birches have been swung , their crimson leaves scattered carelessly , when crystals splint shallow ponds and old egrets stand dark watch the coming dawn , long-legged , knowing how winter is thin , when the first phase transition of water to ice forms slight solidity across meadow streams , small creatures of flesh and concept tiptoe gingerly to some far side where , perhaps , something new is to be found .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA We have lacked a physical definition of an autonomous agent , able to manipulate the universe on its own behalf the egret whose foreboding of winter leads to lifted wing and steady , powerful flight .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The egret is as much a part of physical reality as the atom , and perhaps more than the vaunted quark .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But autonomous agents , we who do daily manipulate the world on our own behalf , we to whom ``intentionality '' and ``purpose '' are so inevitably attributed by our common languages , we are , by my definition of autonomous agents , also nothing but physical systems with a peculiar organization of processes and properties .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If the concept of autonomous agents were something like a useful or more , a proper definition of life itself , then autonomous agents span the gap from the merely physical to that new realm of the merely physical where ``purpose ' ' is ascribed by all of us to one another .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Semantics enters with purpose .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA For this to be true , it is not necessary that the carriers of purpose , say , the same bacterium heading upstream in the glucose gradient , be conscious .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I hope my definition of an autonomous agent is useful , an autocatalytic system carrying out a work cycle , now rather broadened by the realization that autonomous agents also do often detect and measure and record displacements of external systems from equilibrium that can be used to extract work , then do extract work , propagating work and constraint construction , from their environment .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Know-how Bring ourselves empathetically and objectively back three billion years to the mixed microbial community flourishing right about where most of us are now , plus or minus a modicum of layers of surface crustal material .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I want to say that the autonomous agents comprising that community had , individually and collectively , the embodied know - how to get on with making a living in the natural games that constituted their world .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Indeed , as I have emphasized before , a biosphere is a self-consistent coconstruction of autonomous agents , ways of making a living , and the search procedures , mutation , recombination , as well as behavioral search open to autonomous agents .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Those means of making a living that were well searched out and mastered by the agents and their search procedures became the kinds of ``jobs ' ' that were widely filled , the abundant niches of the bio-sphere .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA There is in this whole self - constructing system a wider know-how , beyond the know - how of any single autonomous agent spinning eagerly in its microenvironment .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Yet , clearly , the know -how is distributed .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA There is no autonomous agent , no one , who knows how the whole system works , any more than anyone at present knows how the global economic system works in its myriad interactions , deals , steals , hopes , and frustrations .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA What in the world is ``know-how ' ' ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Philosophers distinguish between ``know-how '' and ``know that . ''####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I know how to tie my shoes and am learning how to play jazz drums .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ` ` Know that '' concerns propositions , most conveniently , human propositions .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I know that the moon is they tell me not made of green cheese .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I know that the earth circles the sun , that the earth is roughly spherical , that chairs are used to sit on .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ` ` Know that '' brings with it the standard and nonstandard issues of the truth or falseness of propositions as they report states of the world .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Perhaps higher primates who are trained to manipulate simple symbols with apparent reference to the world also can ``know that '' with respect to propositions .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Unlike ``know that , '' ``know - how ' ' does not involve propositions about the world .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA `` Know-how '' involves procedural knowledge about how to get on in the world .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The cheetah streaking after the wildebeest , the athletic genius high jumping , have the know -how to do it .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Does a bacterium know how to make a living in its world ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I certainly want to say yes , without attributing consciousness in any way .####[([0], [3], [1], 'Neutral', None)]
NA Watch the myriad subtle turnings on and o of genes , metabolic switching , mechanical twitching , sensing of glucose gradient , swimming and tumbling upstream to higher glucose concentrations .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It knows how all right , even if it cannot talk about how it gets on with its business .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But then , try to talk about tying your shoes or the skilled driving when you become aware some dozens of miles down the road that you have accomplished the tasks without paying the slightest focused attention .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Thank God for know-how .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Know that is a thin veneer on a four-billion - year - old know - how skill abundant in the biosphere .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But any autonomous agent proliferating alone or in a congery of other agents , it would seem , is also graced by the selfsame know-how .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If we synthesize autonomous agents in the next decades and they coevolve under our rapt gaze over months or years into a modestly complex ecosystem brimming with novel life forms , they too will know how to make a living in their mutually created world plus the boundary conditions we more or less intelligently impose on them .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The know- how is , in these terms , nothing but another view of the propagating closures of catalysis , work tasks , sensing , recording , and acting that we now recognize as inherent in the doings of autonomous agents .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The know - how is not outside that propagating organization .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The know-how is the propagating organization .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Semantics####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA All of which brings us , inevitably , to the brink of semantics .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It is simple at its roots , you see .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA An incoming molecular species arriving in the interior of an autonomous agent really is ( i ) food ; ( ii ) poison ; ( iii ) a signal ; ( iv ) neutral ; ( v ) something else .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Once there is an autonomous agent , there is a semantics from its privileged point of view .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The incoming molecule is ``yuck '' or ``yum . ''####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I think the major conceptual step to yuck or yum is unavoidable once there is an autonomous agent .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA And I think we have roughly the Darwinian criteria in mind .####[([0], [3], [2], 'Neutral', 'Average')]
NA If yum , then there will probably be more of this type of agent , osprings of the first .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If yuck , it is not so likely this lineage will prosper .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Once yuck and yum , we are not far from C. S. Pierce ' s meaning - laden semiotic triad : sign , signified , significans .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Like it or not , the glucose gradient is a sign , a predictor , of ``more glucose that way . ''####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Granted , the glucose is not an arbitrary symbol , any more than a cloud is an arbitrary symbol of rain .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In this restricted sense , signs are causally correlated with that which is signified .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA By contrast , the relation between the word ``chair '' and that which it signifies , and on which I am now sitting , is arbitrary .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But can chemical signals in bacterial and plant and human communities be arbitrary from a chemical causal point of view ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If so , can ``mere chemicals ' ' be signs in the full Piercean sense ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I believe it is clear that mere chemistry in an autonomous agent can harbor symbols and signs in the full senses of the words .####[([3, 24], [2], [1], 'Neutral', 'Average')]
NA Consider first the famous genetic code .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Triplets of nucleotides in an RNA molecule stand for specific amino acids that will end up incorporated into a protein .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The detailed causal machinery involves transfer RNA molecules with their anticodon site and the distant site to which amino acids are attached , the aminoacyle transferase enzymes that charge the amino acid binding site of each transfer RNA with the proper amino acid among the twenty amino acids , the binding of the charged transfer RNA ' s anticodon site to the proper RNA code word triplet , the ribosome that glides between adjacent charged transfer RNA molecules and links the successive amino acids into the growing polypeptide chain that hangs free in the cytoplasm , tethered by the ribosome to the messenger RNA molecule as it is ``translated .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ' '####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The arbitrariness of the genetic code is exemplified by the evolution of novel transfer RNA molecules , which translate a given messenger RNA code word triplet into a dierent amino acid .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA As J. Monod properly emphasized three decades ago in a slightly dierent context concerning activation and inhibition of enzymes at allosteric sites on the enzyme that are distant from the catalytic site , the relation of chemical structures that achieve control of catalysis are utterly arbitrary with respect to the chemical structures that undergo the catalysis .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The same is true of the transfer RNA where the anticodon site is distant from the amino acid binding site .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Because of this , which amino acid is charged onto a particular transfer RNA is utterly arbitrary and controlled by the aminoacyle transferase enzyme that does the charging , plus the structure of the amino acid binding site on the transfer RNA .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Both of these can be altered without altering the anticodon-codon matching mechanism .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In short , chemistry allows arbitrary organizations of control relations .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It seems fully legitimate to assign the concepts of sign , signified , and significans to the genetic code .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It seems legitimate to extend that notion to much of the subtle signaling , chemical and otherwise , within and between autonomous agents , as exemplified by plants that upon infestation by a particular insect secrete a secondary metabolite chemical that ``warns ' ' other members of the same species that an insect infestation is happening and to turn on defensive anti-insect secondary metabolites .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The calculus that is Claude Shannon ' s elegant information theory has always been about reduction of uncertainty about the statistics of the source of a set of symbols .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Nowhere in the core of Shannon ' s work concerning the encoding and transmission of information does the meaning , or semantics , of the information enter .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA This is no criticism , and is widely known and appreciated .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA There is , however , just a hint of semantics in Shannon ' s view that the semantics resides in the ``decoder . ''####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I cannot buy Shannon ' s view unless the decoder is an autonomous agent .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If not , then the decoder merely transforms a bit string sent along a communication channel into some other discrete or continuous dynamics perhaps a set of water - filled bowls is drained by turning on a machine that opens valves between the bowls and to the outside world in particular ways .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The patterns of bowl drainage upon receipt of the binary string messages sent along the communication channel constitutes the decoding .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But if the recipient is an autonomous agent such as a bacterium and the incoming molecule is a symbol-sign of a paramecium or an amoeba on the roam and the bacterium swims away and avoids becoming dinner , that sequence of events seems laden with semantics .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If only the bacterium could tell us : ` ` Did you see that truck of a paramecium coming at me ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I ' ve run into that one before !####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I ducked under a boulder , and he never sensed me .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I made it home .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Pass me some more glucose please , Martha . ''####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I will return in the next chapter to discuss such stories , for I will say that we cannot prestate the configuration space of a biosphere and , therefore , cannot deduce that which will unfold .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Thus , among other things , we must tell stories to understand the oriented actions of agents in their worlds .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Do not be overly quick to accuse me of anthropomorphizing .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I too know the risks , including the common claim that we can always in principle translate from ``intentional talk '' to the fully predictive causal account of the events in question .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But patience .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Not only are we unable to prestate the configuration space of a biosphere and predict what will unfold , but we also cannot even translate in the sense of necessary and sucient conditions from legal talk to normal intentional talk , let alone from legal talk of Henderson found guilty of murder to a physical talk about sound -wave forms monitored and masses at space - time lines as a description .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Then let ' s just be naive for the moment .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The semantics of the yuck or yum coming into a simple autonomous agent say , an early bacterium is somehow linked with the embodied know - how of that agent in making a living , or failing to make a living , in its world .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The semantics of an event is some subset of the fully embroidered , context - dependent set of causal implications of the event , or signal , in question .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ` ` For want of a nail , the shoe was lost ; for want of the shoe , the horse was lost ; and for want of the horse , the rider was lost , '' more or less , said Benjamin Franklin .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The semantics of the nail is some subset of this embroidered context- dependent set of implications of the event , or signal , in question to the autonomous agents in the coevolving system .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It seems hard to ascribe purpose , in the sense of acting on its own behalf , to a stone or a chair and easy with respect to an alga .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Of course , there is a sense in which my attribution of semantics to autonomous agents is purely tautological .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA After all , I began by stating that a bacterium swimming upstream in the glucose gradient was acting on its own behalf in an environment , defined an autonomous agent as a physical system able to act on its own behalf , then asked what a physical system must be such that it can act on its own behalf .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Now , five chapters later , it is hardly an independent deduction that autonomous agents are the proposed organization of matter , energy , and organization to which purposes can be ascribed in the sense of being able to act on their own behalf .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA My definition is a definitional circle .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA On the other hand , while the definition is circular , like F = MA and Darwin ' s ``natural selection '' and ``fitness , '' that does not mean that the set of codefined concepts surrounding my definition of an autonomous agent as a reproducing system that does a work cycle fails to touch the real world .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Stones and chairs are not , by my definition , autonomous agents .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA All living cells are .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA And the stunning fact directly before us , every day , is that autonomous agents do manipulate the world on their own behalf .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Watch a pair of nesting birds build their nest .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In short , once we have autonomous agents and yuck and yum , it appears that semantics enters the universe as the agents coevolve and behave on their own behalf with one another in the unfolding of a biosphere .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Knowing####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA What about ``knowing '' ? Daniel Dennett , in his fine book Darwin ' s Dangerous Idea , advances a hierarchy of forms of ``knowing , '' if I may use that term , that have arisen in evolution by Darwinian means .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I find his hierarchy congenial and informative .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Dennett envisions evolution as a sequence of kinds of construction cranes that bit by bit build up higher - order entities via variation and natural selection .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I do not disagree , although I have placed far greater emphasis on the roles of self-organization in evolution .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Here , in Investigations , I am trying to point at the mysterious but utterly natural hopefulness in which an increasing diversity of broken symmetries in the universe creates the diversity of structures and processes that can constitute and identify ramified and ramifying sources of energy , detect those sources of energy , create devices and processes that couple to those sources of energy , and generate yet more diversity that propagates macroscopic order even further .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I wonder , in short , at the naturalness and self- generaticity of Dennett ' s cranes building cranes building cranes in biospheres , perhaps planetary geologies , and beyond .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But back to the past .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Dennett distinguishes ` `Darwinian creatures , '' ` `Pavlovian creatures , '' ` `Popperian creatures , '' and ``Gregorian creatures . ''####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA A simple autonomous agent , say , a bacterium , is a Darwinian creature .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In its simplest version , the creature evolves by mutation , also recombination and natural selection .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA For the moment , no behavioral learning is to be considered .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA So one ( or a colony or an ecosystem ) of Darwinian creatures adapts more or less as Darwin told us .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA At the next level up , say , aplysia , a nervous system is present , and the creature is capable of stimulus - response learning , a la Pavlov .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Indeed , aplysia can learn very simple conditioned stimuli the later analogue is the bell causing the dog to salivate in ``expectation '' of food .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA At the next level ( Dennett , perhaps properly , reserves this for us vertebrates ) is the Popperian creature .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Popperian creatures , in Dennett ' s fine phrase , have ``internal models '' of their world and can ``run the internal model ' ' with the clutch disengaged , rather than running the model in real time in the real world .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA This allows us lucky Popperian creatures to allow our ``hypotheses to die in our stead . ''####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I love that image .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Beyond the Popperian is the Gregorian creature namely , at least humans .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Dennett makes the wonderful argument that we utilize our tools literally stone knives , arrows , digging sticks , machine tools to enlarge our shared world of facts and processes .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA This enlarged shared world gives us more know-how , and more know that .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Cultural evolution , at some point , begins to burst out -of-bounds .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Hard rock music jangles the minarets of Iran .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Who knows what new cultural forms will blossom ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Chinese cooking lands in Cuba , and Cuban - Chinese cuisine is invented .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA What ' s next under the sun ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Who can say ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I very much like Dennett ' s ladder of know-how , and eventual know that .####[([5, 15], [2, 4], [1], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA Without invoking consciousness , not because it is not worth invoking but because so little sensible has ever been said on the subject , it seems worth asking how much of this hierarchy could be realized by simple molecular systems , even without evoking nerve cells .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I would think a lot of this hierarchy could find molecular realizations .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA For example , bacteria and amoebae do have a kind of Pavlovian learning already , for they have receptors that accommodate to a constant level of a given signal ligand and sense instead a change from the current level .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA This is not yet the association of a more or less arbitrary conditioned stimulus with an unconditioned stimulus , but I can imagine chemistry to accomplish the latter .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA As neurons are supposed to proliferate and form novel synaptic connections that survive if used and to mediate the linkage of conditioned to unconditioned stimulus , why not envision a complex chemistry , say , very complex carbohydrate -synthesis patterns sustained by complex sets of enzymes whose activities are modulated by the dierent carbohydrates themselves , which is true of contemporary carbohydrate metabolism .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Such a system might blindly try out variant patterns of synthesis until it could establish a self-sustaining web linking the carbohydrates , the enzymes , and certain protein receptors mediating the linkage between unconditioned and conditioned stimulus , then maintain that linkage by positive feedback loops .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The image is not too far from how it is imagined that ``idiotype ' ' and ``anti-idiotype '' immune networks work to sustain synthesis of a set of desired antibodies against an incoming pathogen .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In such networks , for which there is modestly good evidence , a given first antibody serves as an antigen that stimulates the body to produce a second antibody that binds to the unique amino acid sequences , called the ``idiotype ' ' of the first antibody .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In turn , the second ``anti-idiotype ' ' antibody stimulates a third , which stimulates a fourth .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But this series is likely to form feedback loops because the first and third antibody can often both bind to the same site on the second antibody , hence , the first and third antibodies are similar shapes in shape space .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It is not much of a stretch to think of the immune system as a conditioned stimulus response system .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Popperian creatures ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Why cannot the molecular-sensing and hypothesis-testing churning concerns of the bacterium as it senses a paramecium churn twenty cycles before kicking in the rotary motor , or not , such that the wee bacterium hides under a boulder of a grain of sand until the beast passes by ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Are nerves necessary ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Plants , as noted , are said to signal one another with complex secondary metabolites to characterize the particular kinds of insects infesting the glade .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA There are arbitrary structural relations between the metabolite and the insect , just as symbols in human language are often arbitrary with respect to the signified .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Not bad for nerveless nonvertebrates .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I do get stuck at Gregorian creatures .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Even here , the free and open creating of new symbol strings in a language , wherever new sentences can be created , is not that fundamentally dierent from the persistent open creation of new kinds of molecules in the biosphere as a whole .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If the conversation we recent two -legged ones are having with respect to our digging sticks and atomic bombs is impressive , so too is the chemical conversation in any full-fledged ecosystem , where we are all instrumental in the lives of one another .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I suppose I am naively driven to consider that the biosphere , with its urgent diversity in which , emboldened by all our know - how , we do get on with a very rich conversation , may very early already have harbored all the levels of which Dennett speaks .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA We humans are just more gregarious with our vocal cords and e-mail , I guess .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Smart place , a biosphere , lots to talk about .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Four billion years of yammering .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Slapstick comedy may have started a long time ago .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Ethics####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA And what of ethics ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Does a whi of ethical issue arise with autonomous agents ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Yuck or yum from my point of view if I am an autonomous agent .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA There are deep reasons for caution .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Hume told us long ago about the ``naturalistic fallacy '' :####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA One cannot deduce ``ought '' from ``is . ''####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA From the fact that mothers care for their young , we cannot deduce that they ought to do so , Hume argued .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA From the fact that Hitler set out to conquer Europe and more and to kill Jewry , we cannot deduce that he ought to have done so .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Indeed , Hume ' s injunction underlies the caution of scientists about making ethical statements .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA We scientists find the facts .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA You citizens across the globe can argue the ethics .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But if Hume warns us not to deduce ought from is , where do values come from at all ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Hume ' s injunction against deduction from is to ought nevertheless began by recognizing the legitimacy of the category ``ought . ''####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The eorts following Hume to understand the meaning of ethical assertions have been long , twisted , arduous .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Following the dictates of the logical positivists of the Vienna Circle that only those statements capable of verification were meaningful , philosophers as famous as G. E. Moore came to wonder if ethical assertions were merely emotive utterances .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ` ` It is wrong to kill . ''####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Becomes , ``Agggah ! ''####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Does the positivist argument seem persuasive ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It has always amused me that the core injunction of the logical positivists , ``only those statements that are empirically verifiable are meaningful , '' is itself not empirically verifiable .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA One is reminded of something about hoisting and petards .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA John Rawls of Harvard has argued eloquently that our human notions of fairness derive from what we would all ``contractually '' agree to , were we to know before birth that we would all be born with diering abilities and endowments .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Thus ``equality before the law '' is one contract that Rawls commends to us .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA `` Equality before the law '' is far more refined than the yuck or yum of the bacterium .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The emergence of ethics in the evolution of life on this planet is a fascinating issue .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I will content myself with wondering where ``value '' and the rudiments of ``intentionality '' come from in the physical universe in the first place and leave social contracts for other eorts .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Where is the place of value in a world of fact ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Too much yuck , this one and its progeny are gone from the future of the biosphere .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Without attributing consciousness to an E. coli , or an autonomous agent we may create in the near future , I cannot help but feel that the rudiments of value are present once autonomous agents are around .####[([1, 19], [25], [21], 'Neutral', 'Average')]
NA And again without attributing consciousness , once an autonomous agent is around is the rudiment of intentionality present ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If so , another cornerstone of ethical activity has been laid .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Ethical behavior requires first the logical possibility of behavior for which one is responsible .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA But what are ``acts '' in the first place ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Daniel Yamins is a brilliant young mathematician .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Now entering Harvard , Dan spent a summer with me at the Santa Fe Institute before he learned to drive , after an earlier summer spent in the laboratory of Jack Szostak at Harvard , where , at age fourteen , Dan was learning to evolve RNA molecules to bind arbitrary ligands .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Hamburg -- Some 200 German Border Guard officers working in cooperation with the Hamburg prosecutors ' office on Wednesday cracked a ring of Afghan smugglers who have been operating throughout Europe .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Officials say that the smuggling ring had been illegally bringing fellow nationals into Germany via Austria since at least October 2001 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Many of the refugees then travelled by rail from Hamburg to Britain via Brussels .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Others took trains , vans and cars onto ferries destined for Scandinavia .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Afghans paid gang members up to 9,000 euros ( $ 7,900 ) to make the trip .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The border guard officers searched a total of 16 apartments , stores and offices downtown and in Hamburg 's Altona , Billstedt , Schnelsen , and Harburg districts , detaining 14 suspects .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA An arrest warrant for the suspected leader of the gang , an Afghan , was also served .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Police seized 33,9000 euros -- believed to be earnings from smuggling operations -- in the apartment of the 35 - year - old suspected ringleader .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Two men who were working with him , an Afghan and a Pakistani , were arrested as well .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Eleven others were taken into custody , seven of whom were also members of the smuggling ring .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The remaining four turned out to be Afghan refugees .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA A further four suspects were arrested in a similar operation in Frankfurt .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Police interrogators were told the refugees had been " parked " and were working illegally in northern Germany until they could be moved to other locations .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Sites in the towns of Ratzeburg and Uelzen were also searched in connection with the raid , said Wieland Mozdzynski , director of the Hamburg office of the border guard .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Mr. Mozdzynski said that during the operation , which stretched as far as the state of Bavaria and Austria , police had uncovered an " international network of groups , each with specific tasks . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA He added that the groups worked independently , but exploited existing contacts regularly .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA According to a police spokesman , more than 500 officers took part in the joint operation .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Another officer said the loose structure of the smuggling ring made the investigation more difficult .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA He said that the bust was nevertheless a significant and successful strike against gangs and businesses engaged in human smuggling .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA The charge represents a write-down of the goodwill associated with Poughkeepsie 's investment in the banks it is trying to sell and its North Carolina branches as well .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The thrift announced the plan Aug. 21 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA After their withdrawal from Bethlehem , Bayt Jala , and Qalqilya , the Israeli forces withdrew from Ramallah yesterday , but they maintained the siege and closure around the city .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA This means that the suffering of the citizens in Ramallah , like the suffering of the citizens in Bethlehem , Bayt Jala , and Qalqilya , will continue on the roadblocks , affecting their medical , economic , educational , and social life .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA No other people in the world have seen such suffering .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The main and perhaps only reason for this suffering is the continuing Israeli occupation and its heavy burden on Palestinian citizens .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Israeli withdrawal was a correction of a mistake the Israeli Government made when it decided to reoccupy parts of the main West Bank cities following the assassination of Israeli minister Rehav'am Ze'evi .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The reoccupation was a kind of collective punishment for the inhabitants of those cities and the villages around them , villages that constitute an organic and vital extension of the cities .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Israeli forces destroyed buildings and installations in those cities , arrested dozens of citizens , and killed dozens others .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA That showed that the ruling right-wing coalition in Israel is pursuing an occupational policy and is not , in the first place , willing to recognize the firm national Palestinian rights to freedom , independence , and the end of occupation and settlement .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA This policy , which disregards the need to establish a just peace based on the need for the Palestinian people to regain their freedom and independence , is reflected in statements made by the Israeli officials , who brag about the large number of Palestinians who were killed or arrested by the Israeli forces .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It is also reflected in the fact that the ruling Israeli coalition has no agreed -upon political plan and that the settlement plans and initiatives that are attributed to this Israeli official or that are unable to meet the minimum legitimate Palestinian demands .####[([0], [43], [42], 'Neutral', 'Average')]
NA These initiatives and plans largely try to keep as much hegemony and as many settlements as possible on Palestinian lands , resources , airspace , and crossing points .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In its approach to the national Palestinian rights the Israeli Government is playing the cat and mouse game .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It is trying to use the time factor to perpetuate the occupation .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It is also working to push the Palestinians and the world into new labyrinths and tunnels , inside the old tunnels , to distract them from the main and central demands .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The cycle of reoccupation - withdrawal - reoccupation is part of this approach , which is no secret to anyone .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The only way to peace lies in the full Israeli withdrawal from the Palestinian territories that were occupied in 1967 and the termination of the occupational and settlement presence in these territories .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The way to peace does not lie in devious methods to circumvent the inalienable Palestinian rights .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Such methods would only complicate things and add fuel to the raging fire .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Many Little Sisters are preparing to go back to school this fall full of hope and with a positive outlook .####[([0], [13, 20], [1, 3], 'Positive', 'Strong')]
NA Thanks to our Big Sisters volunteers , these young people are self-confident , believe in themselves and are beginning to realize their full potential .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA A recent study bypositive Public / Private Ventures ( PPV ) showed that girls who had a Big Sister for just one year : reduced first - time drug use by 46 % lowered school absenteeism by 52 % cut violent behavior by 33 % enhanced school performance showed improved peer and family relationships Former Little Sister Amy , now 18 - years old , is a testament to the Big Sisters program .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " I was matched with my Big Sister in June of 1992 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Since then , she and I have grown very close and I have been able to experience lots of new things .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA We go to movies , dinner , concerts , and other stuff like that , but I have also been able to participate in charity events and fundraiser type things .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Not only did I have a lot of fun with my Big Sister , but I learned a lot from her too .####[([0], [5, 9], [0], 'Positive', 'Strong')]
NA I have become more open-minded , more responsible , and , most importantly , I have gained a lot more self-confidence .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I am very thankful to the Big Sisters program for allowing me this very special opportunity .####[([6, 9], [3, 4], [0], 'Positive', 'Strong')]
NA In 1998 , Big Sisters served 972 young people through its many programs .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But the need is still great .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Over 170 young people are still waiting for a mentor .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA INDUSTRY####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA During the first ten months of 2001 , 129.1 billion hryvnyas ' worth of industrial goods were produced ( services rendered ) .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Compared with the corresponding period last year , output volumes grew 16.1 % .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Increases in production were achieved in all regions of the country and in all the principal forms of industrial activity .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In the extractive industry production volumes increased 4.1 % since the beginning of the year as compared with the same period last year .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In the manufacturing industry , which accounts for nearly three - quarters of all industrial production , output volumes increased 19.6 % over the course of the first ten months of 2001 as against the corresponding period last year .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Output volumes in the food industry and in the processing of agricultural products rose 19.8 % as compared with January - October of last year .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Light industry achieved an increase of 15.9 % in output during the reporting period .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Production in the textile industry grew 12 % .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA At enterprises that process wood and manufacture wood products , output volumes increased 25.9 % during the first ten months of the current year as compared with the same period last year .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In the pulp and paper industry , production volumes rose 20.5 % as compared with the corresponding period last year .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Output volumes at metallurgical and metal - processing enterprises increased 8.3 % since the beginning of the current year .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Output volumes at enterprises that produce coke and the products of oil refining increased 57.1 % .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In the chemical and petrochemical industry , the increase in production during the period since the beginning of the current year amounted to 11.9 % .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Compared with January - October of last year , output volumes at enterprises that generate and distribute electric power grew by 2.4 % .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA During the reporting period , 138 billion kWh of electric power were produced , which was one billion kWh ( 0.7 % ) more power than during January - October 2000 , despite a 3.7 - percent reduction of output of electric power by nuclear power station .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA The right- wing Peronist party Partido Justicialista ( Justice Party ) has won the elections of Sunday 14th October for the Argentine Senate and Chamber of Deputies with an absolute majority .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The results of the elections were to be expected in view of the catastrophic economic situation of the majority of the country 's citizens .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Argentina has an ever-growing rate of poverty , which defies logic given the enormous land / population ratio , with the richest soil in South America .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Once again , the governing class of a South American country has proved itself utterly unable to come to terms with the needs of the population , basically because it has become removed from the reality of the country .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The more the poles part , the further the political and social distance between the parts .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The fact that a right-wing party has conquered an absolute majority in Argentina proves the desperation of the people , although 41 % of the population voted with spoiled or void votes .####[([0], [16, 17], [18, 19], 'Negative', 'Strong')]

NA ZIMBABWE is amassing huge quantities of arms and ammunition using two African allies in preparation for next year 's crucial presidential election , it has been established .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Financial Gazette investigations in the past one - and - a- half months have revealed that the Democratic Republic of the Congo ( DRC ) and Namibia are helping Zimbabwe circumvent an international arms embargo to buy huge quantities of guns and bullets for next year 's ballot .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The arms embargo was imposed on Harare last year by Europe and the United States on President Robert Mugabe 's government because of its appalling human rights record .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The investigations show that Zimbabwe is importing and massing an assortment of guns at army bases around the country in preparation for the poll , which is expected to be violent .####[([0], [27, 28], [0], 'Neutral', 'Weak')]
NA Most of the guns have been arriving secretly at Suri Suri airbase in Chegutu before they are distributed to other military bases and some will be sent to farms where self-styled war veterans have established bases to intimidate voters .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The bulk of the weapons have arrived from the DRC in that country 's military cargo plane .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The weapons consist of a significant portion of French - made guns , most of which top government sources say will be distributed to war veterans who are central to the ruling ZANU PF party 's re-election strategy in the presidential poll .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The sources say Zimbabwe , after the massive depletion of its armoury because of its participation in the three - year- old DRC war , has been finding it extremely difficult to replenish its arms stocks because its traditional and cheaper arms suppliers in Europe are refusing to sell it arms .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA This had forced the army to implement some unpalatable measures , including the grounding of most of its entire fleet of Hawk fighter aircraft due to Britain 's refusal to sell spare parts .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Virtually all European Union member states have severed ties with Zimbabwe and imposed an arms embargo on the country .####[([11], [7, 9], [1, 6], 'Negative', 'Average')]
NA " Although we can still buy a number of arms from countries like Russia and China , a greater part of our fairly priced weapons , ammunition and spares have been sourced from mainly European countries like Britain , Sweden , France and others over the years .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA We can no longer buy arms from Europe at the moment because of the problems here , " said a top Ministry of Defence source .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " We have been left with no alternative but to buy some weapons via our allies in the DRC who have access to some of these European weapons that we have preference for . "####[([24, 28], [31, 33], [0], 'Positive', 'Average')]

NA I am not going to comment on that one , " Sekeramayi said yesterday before immediately cutting off his telephone .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA We have , for instance , sold arms to many French - speaking countries .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Billions of investors ' dollars are pouring out of the nation 's junk - bond mutual funds , undermining a pillar of support in the already reeling junk market .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Last week alone , an eye-popping $ 1.6 billion flowed out of the junk funds , or nearly 5 % of their total assets , according to estimates by Dalbar Financial Services Inc. , a Boston research firm .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In the past two months the nation 's 88 junk funds have lost a total of about $ 6 billion -- more than 15 % of assets -- through sales or transfers of junk - fund shares , Dalbar says .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It made the estimates based on data collected from more than a dozen big junk funds .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Interviews with three major fund groups -- Fidelity Investments , Vanguard Group Inc. and T. Rowe Price Associates Inc. -- confirm the trend .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Their junk funds combined have had net outflows totaling nearly $ 500 million , or about 13 % of their junk fund assets , in the past two months .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Some fund managers say negative publicity has exacerbated investors ' concern about recent declines in junk - bond prices .####[([13, 19], [11], [1, 3], 'Negative', 'Average')]
NA " People have been seeing headline after headline after headline and saying : ` I ca n't take it anymore -- I 'm getting out , ' " says Kurt Brouwer of Brouwer & Janachowski , a San Francisco investment adviser .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The withdrawals could spell trouble for the $ 200 billion junk market .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If the heavy outflows continue , fund managers will face increasing pressure to sell off some of their junk to pay departing investors in the weeks ahead .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Such selling could erode prices of high- yield junk bonds , already weakened by a rash of corporate credit problems .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Mutual fund groups have n't lost control of much of the outgoing money , says Louis Harvey , Dalbar 's president .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Mutual fund officials say that investors have transferred most of it into their money market accounts , and to a lesser extent , government - bond funds .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA So the impact on the $ 950 billion mutual fund industry as a whole probably will be slight .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But tremors are likely in the junk- bond market , which has helped to finance the takeover boom of recent years .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Contact was made on Saturday between outer space and the Free State city of Bloemfontein when President Thabo Mbeki spoke to Africa 's first astronaut Mark Shuttleworth , aboard the International Space Station .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Speaking via a live satellite link from Bloemfontein , the president praised the so-called " Afronaut " for his contribution to science and Africa 's renaissance .####[([19, 26], [12], [10, 11], 'Positive', 'Strong')]
NA " Yes ambassador , how are you ? "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Mbeki started the 10 - minute conversation , broadcast live at the Free State rugby stadium .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Shuttleworth described his journey so far as very exciting , saying the flight had been smooth and everything was going according to plan .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " I have had moments of terror and moments of sheer exhilaration , " he proclaimed .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " I have never seen anything as beautiful as earth from space .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I cannot imagine anything as beautiful as that . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The 28 - year- old Internet millionaire said he was sleeping comfortably , and the food was not too bad either .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA He showed the president an empty tin of what had contained his lunch - pork and potato .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " So far , we 've only come to try the Russian food , which was tasty .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA I am sure the American food will be just as good , " Shuttleworth told the president .####[([4, 6], [2, 3], [14], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA He also reported that he had started setting up for several scientific experiments he was planning to do on board the ISS .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Mbeki expressed South Africa 's pride at Shuttleworth 's efforts , saying they would go a long way towards inspiring young people to take up subjects like engineering , mathematics and science .####[([8, 10], [6], [1], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA Shuttleworth agreed that this was essential towards Africa 's rebirth .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA He said he had seen the most magnificent sunset and sunrise over Africa , at which Mbeki asked him to bring pictures " so that we can know what we look like to you from up there " .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA South Africans should be looking up smiling when he returns , Shuttleworth replied .####[([0], [7], [12], 'Positive', 'Average')]

NA Source : Sapa / mlr / shob Date : 27 Apr 2002 14:16####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Beijing has completed the afforestation of 4,000 hectares over the past six months , the municipal forestry bureau revealed yesterday .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " We planted trees mainly in the major five areas that are severely endangered by sandy wind , " said Cai Baojun , an official with the bureau in charge of forest planting .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The shifting dunes in Beijing 's suburbs and rural areas have been successfully controlled by green barriers of trees and grass , which have also helped upgrade the city 's forest proportion to 43 per cent , 23 percentage points higher than the nation 's metropolitan average .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA A 200 - metre belt of trees has been planted on each side of the Yongding , Chaobai , Dasha and Wenyu rivers , which was previously the city 's most desertificated land .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Forestry experts said dry weather and temperature fluctuations were the main cause of sandstorms .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The repeated breaching of the embankments of the Yongding and Chaobai rivers also resulted in the desertification of the land with heavy sand being deposited by floods .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA By 2005 , 50 per cent of Beijing 's land , including both urban and rural areas , will have been covered with trees .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The green belts have helped protect the crops from sand , wind , drought and floods to guarantee grain production , Cai said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Over the next 10 years , China will invest 6 billion yuan ( US $ 720 million ) to prevent sandstorms hitting Beijing , according to sources from the State Forestry Administration .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Private organizations are also being encouraged to help fight sandstorms , according to the administration 's vice-director Li Yucai .####[([8, 10], [3, 6], [18, 19], 'Positive', 'Weak')]
NA Favourable taxation policies will also be given to people engaged in the transformation of desertificated land .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Beijing was struck by sandstorms several times this spring .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It is believed that sand from northern areas , especially the Inner Mongolia Autonomous Region , and floating dust from the city 's uncovered construction sites are the main causes .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Rumsfeld Defends U.S. Treatment of Detainees in Cuba####[([3, 7], [2], [1], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA WASHINGTON , Jan. 22 - Frustrated by an international outcry over the American treatment of prisoners in Cuba , Secretary of Defense Donald H. Rumsfeld defended the United States ' conduct at length today and dismissed the criticism as breathless armchair hyperbole .####[([8, 18], [6], [20, 25], 'Negative', 'Strong'), ([27, 31], [26], [20, 25], 'Positive', 'Average'), ([37, 38], [36], [20, 25], 'Negative', 'Weak'), ([12, 18], [38], [20, 25], 'Negative', 'Strong'), ([12, 18], [10], [20, 25], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA " I am telling you what I believe in every inch of my body to be the truth , and I have spent a lot of time on secure video with the people down there , " he told reporters , referring to the United States naval base at Guantanamo Bay , Cuba , where 158 prisoners from the war in Afghanistan are being jailed .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " I have n't found a single scrap of any kind of information that suggests that anyone has been treated anything other than humanely . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Mr. Rumsfeld spoke in an unusual briefing that stretched over an hour in an attempt , he said , to " tap down some of this hyperbole . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It was prompted by a rising tide of international criticism after the Defense Department released photographs over the weekend that showed some of the prisoners kneeling before their captors , their legs in shackles , their hands bound in manacles , their mouths covered by surgical masks and their eyes blinded by large goggles with black tape .####[([12, 14], [5, 10], [9], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA His comments came as criticism swelled from abroad .####[([0], [5, 6], [8], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA Critics said the United States was using sensory deprivation and other psychological control techniques to weaken the prisoners so that interrogations would be more fruitful .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The International Committee of the Red Cross , in a rare break with its code of not publicly criticizing detaining governments , said the United States might have violated Geneva Convention rules against making a spectacle of prisoners by distributing the pictures , which were published worldwide .####[([34, 38], [32, 33], [1, 7], 'Negative', 'Weak')]
NA Amnesty International sought access to the prisoners in Guantanamo and said they should be allowed to have lawyers .####[([4, 9], [3], [1, 2], 'Positive', 'Weak')]
NA " Keeping prisoners incommunicado , sensory deprivation , the use of unnecessary restraint and the humiliation of people through tactics such as shaving them are all classic techniques employed to break the spirit of individuals ahead of interrogation , " the organization said .####[([0], [16, 17], [41, 42], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA Several governments joined the chorus , saying the prisoners should be granted prisoner of war status under the Geneva Convention .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Such status would accord them the highest level of protections .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Javier Solana , the European Union foreign policy chief , said that despite the Sept. 11 atrocities , " changing our values and our way of life would be terrorism 's first victory . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Netherlands also urged Washington to recognize the detainees as prisoners of war , saying , " In the fight , we need to uphold our norms and values . "####[([5, 13], [4], [1, 2], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA While debate raged elsewhere , Britain and Spain supported the United States .####[([10, 12], [9], [6, 8], 'Positive', 'Weak')]
NA Prime Minister Tony Blair 's office said the three British prisoners at the detention center , called Camp X -Ray , " had no complaints about their treatment . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Spanish Foreign Minister Josep Pique said the Spanish government " does not have the slightest doubt regarding the position of the U.S. government . "####[([18, 23], [11, 16], [1, 5], 'Positive', 'Strong')]
NA The warden at Camp X-Ray , Col .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Terry Carrico , said he was determined at all times to maintain what he called " positive control " over the prisoners .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Bill Nash , a retired Army major general and senior fellow at the Council on Foreign Relations , said this amounted to " imposing on them a psychological sense of isolation , domination and futility , and trying to establish the conditions by which you can then reward them for information , as oppose to punish them . "####[([0], [28, 35], [1, 2], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA Mr. Rumsfeld said it was " probably unfortunate " that the photographs were released , at least without an explanation .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA He said the prisoners had been photographed in a holding area just before their restraints were removed and they were put in their cages .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " If you want to think the worst about things , you can , " he said .####[([5, 10], [4], [16], 'Positive', 'Average'), ([10], [5, 8], [16], 'Negative', 'Average')]
NA But he argued that whenever prisoners , especially those who are dangerous and suicidal , are transported , it only makes sense to lock them in restraints .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " When they are being moved from place to place , will they be restrained in a way so that they are less likely to be able to kill an American soldier ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA You bet .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA No .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Yes . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It is not clear why the United States has not officially designated the detainees as prisoners of war , especially since Mr. Rumsfeld said they are essentially being treated as such .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA A three - day workshop on money laundering started on Monday , with the participation of officials from several Arab banks , discussing the impact and size of this problem in the Middle East .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA During the workshop , organised by the Union of Arab Banks ( UAB ) , participants will also review legislation Arab countries have introduced to combat this phenomenon as well as the ways and means by which money is laundered .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Participants will also explore the role of banking and financial institutions in combating money laundering and the American and European approaches to fighting this problem .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA According to UAB Secretary General Fu'ad####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Shakir the size of money laundering worldwide ranges from 2 to 5 per cent of the world 's gross domestic product , which could run up to $ 1.5 trillion .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA He said that banks , real estate , construction projects , stock markets , investing in losing companies and gambling are among the favourite targets for money launderers .####[([4, 20], [21, 24], [1], 'Neutral', 'Average')]
NA The source of this money includes drug trafficking , arms deals and prostitution which are the major sources of what has been termed as " dirty money . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The process of money laundering starts with what has been termed as Placement , or injecting the dirty money into the market , followed by Layering , or removing all traces of the money laundered and finally Integration , where the money becomes " clean " .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Although interest in this issue started in the 1980's , world attention on money laundering intensified following the Sept. 11 attacks in New York and Washington , Shakir , who was addressing the participants , said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA He said that Arab banks and financial institutions were targeted by the anti-terrorism campaign that followed the attacks .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " Our institutions are far away from this money laundering phenomenon and Arab governments have amended banking laws to combat money laundering , " Shakir said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Jordan was among the Arab countries which introduced measures to fight this problem including tightening banking rules and imposing strict controls on money transfers .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Punishment for money laundering was also introduced , illegal money is confiscated and tough jail terms are given to violators .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Money launderers target countries with low risk of detection , soft tax systems and lenient banking regulations , Shakir said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA He said , according to international agencies which combat this phenomenon , statistically the United States ranks first in term of destination , origin and flows of laundered money .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In Europe , Italy and Russia top the list while China ranks first among Asian countries .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA According to Shakir , money laundering in the Arab world is " very minimal " but he said that Lebanon and Egypt are classified by international agencies as among the countries that have not taken necessary measures to combat this problem .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA The second ever case of Bovine Spongiform Encephalopathy ( BSE , mad cow disease ) in Meurthe-et - Moselle [ department in northeast France ] was diagnosed on Monday [ 13 August ] , in Longuyon , in the north of the department , in a cow born in 1994 , the FDSEA [ Departmental Federation of Farmers ' Trade Unions ] announced in a statement .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Charolais breed cow , was part of the GAEC ( Agricultural Cooperative Grouping ) Bruyeres herd in Longuyon , showed signs of the illness and was slaughtered .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The test , which was carried out in conformity with the rules for such cases , raised suspicions of BSE , which were later confirmed .####[([20], [18], [0], 'Negative', 'Weak')]
NA The herd is made up of 220 cattle which will have to be slaughtered , according to the rules .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The first BSE case [ in Meurthe-et- Moselle ] was discovered on 17 July in a Charolais bull , in the south of the department .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Hanoi , Feb. 9 ( VNA ) -- Vietnam and the United States will organize a scientific conference on human health and the environmental effects of Agent Orange / Dioxins in Hanoi's Daewoo Hotel from Mar. 3 -6 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA According to the National Institute of Environment and Health Sciences ( NIEHS ) of the US , the conference will offer scientists worldwide opportunities to exchange scientific information on the effects of Agent Orange / Dioxins on human health and the environment and discuss measures to reduce the hazards of this toxic chemical .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Scientists will evaluate available dioxin-related research results and define present requirements for further research .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA NIEHS said that the conference will mark the start of joint scientific research on the impact of defoliant sprayed by the US Air Force during the war in Vietnam .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It is expected to lay a foundation for further bilateral cooperation projects in this field as well as seeking funding for future projects .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA According to unofficial reports , between 1961 and 1971 , US aircraft sprayed 72 million liters of toxic chemicals , including 44 million liters of Agent Orange , containing 170 kg of dioxin , in Vietnam .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Dioxin is an extremely poisonous chemical that causes cancer , immune system malfunction and birth defects .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA When the US war ended in 1975 , three million Vietnamese had been killed , 4.4 million wounded and two million affected by toxic chemicals , mainly Agent Orange .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In the first decade after the war , about 50,000 children were born with deformities or paralysis to parents affected by toxic chemicals .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA In rand-terms , an additional R7,77 - million was committed for drought relief to bring the total to R44 - million ; R6,48 - million to support the objective of achieving an integrated regional market in southern Africa , bringing the total committed to R189 - million ; and R898560 in support of strengthening regional economies through non governmental organisations , bringing the total committed to the programme to R88,99 - million .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The three programmes are virtually open ended , being topped up as projects finish and others are initiated .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Venezuela 's new dawn####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA BBC correspondent in Caracas####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Venezuelans awoke on Friday to a country transformed by the dramatic and violent events of the last 24 hours , which left at least 11 people dead and more than 80 injured .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA A general strike and an escalating oil industry stoppage that had threatened to cripple the country 's economy were no more - and the country not only had a new president , business leader Pedro Carmona , but a new name .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The country was no longer the Bolivarian Republic of Venezuela , in honour of South American independence hero Simon Bolivar , one of former president Hugo Chavez 's heroes .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Now it is simply the Republic of Venezuela .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The name change was Mr Carmona 's first act as head of the transition government .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Their products , in high quality and great variety , are shipped to supermarkets and hotels and sold at a good price .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA US human rights report termed inaccurate####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ISLAMABAD , March 5 : The government on Tuesday rejected the US State Department Report on human rights as " factually inaccurate and unwarranted " adding that it reflected tendency of some states to sit in judgment on others .####[([11, 18], [10], [6, 7], 'Negative', 'Average')]
NA " The reports fails to acknowledge the important policy measures and initiatives by the government of Pakistan to promote and protect human rights , " said a statement issued by Foreign Office spokesman in which the report was termed as factually inaccurate and unwarranted .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It pointed out that all the goals set at an April 2000 human rights conference had been achieved , which it added had been ignored by the report .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Enlisting these initiatives , it recalled that these include promulgation of the Juvenile Justice System Ordinance , the establishment of a permanent commission on the status of women , police and jail reforms , national policy and plan of action for elimination of child labour and establishment of a fund for rehabilitation of working children .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The government , it added , has amended Pakistan Citizenship Act of 1951 to enable women of Pakistani descent to claim Pakistani nationality for their children born to foreign husbands .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA A mass awareness campaign was launched as part of the observance of the Year 2000 as the year of Human Rights and Human Dignity , it added .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In addition , it said , Pakistan also ratified ILO Conventions 100 on equal remuneration and 182 on the elimination of worst forms of child labour .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It signed the Optional Protocols to Convention on the Rights of Child .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Recently the system of joint electorates has been introduced respecting the wishes of the minority communities , it said .####[([2, 9], [12, 13], [18], 'Neutral', 'Weak')]
NA Despite these developments , the report states " the government 's human rights record remained poor . "####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " This is unacceptable and a gross misstatement of the facts .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The government of Pakistan therefore , feels constrained to reject the assessment of the report about Pakistan , and the tendency of some states to sit in judgment over others . "####[([11, 30], [7, 10], [0], 'Negative', 'Average')]
NA " The cause of human rights would be better served if all states , in a spirit of cooperation and understanding address the problems they face in promoting and protecting human rights , " it said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA Seoul , Nov. 19 ( Yonhap ) --####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The recent settlement of details regarding the Kyoto Protocol is putting local exporters on alert .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Kyoto Protocol was made by members of the United Nations Framework Convention for Climate Change at its seventh session held in Marrakech , Morocco at the start of the month .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If the protocol , which prescribes an obligatory reduction of greenhouse gases , is put into effect , the nation 's export will be heavily damaged .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Kyoto Protocol is an agreement to get 30 leading industrialized countries such as Japan and members of the European Union ( EU ) to lessen greenhouse gas emissions by amounts as high as 95 percent of levels in the 1990 's .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The government and business circle expect the nation 's exports to be damaged in direct and indirect ways from 2008 , when advanced nations will begin to be regulated by the protocol .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The reason is that South Korea 's industrial structure depends heavily on the export of products including not only durable appliances such as air conditioner but also automobiles all of which should meet intensified environmental standards before they can be shipped overseas under the Protocol .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Also , advanced nations are likely to make use of the standards as a new trade barrier .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Moreover , the pressures from advanced countries to get South Korea to cut its greenhouse gas emissions is expected to strengthen .####[([8, 17], [4], [6, 7], 'Neutral', 'Weak')]
NA South Korea ranked ninth on a list of the largest greenhouse gas producers , and Korea 's per-capita emissions were also close to those of advanced countries .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Under this situation , the nation cannot possibly avoid pressures to match the cuts of advanced nations .####[([12, 17], [10], [0], 'Neutral', 'Weak')]
NA In particular , Japan and European countries are likely to persuade developing countries including South Korea to take part in the reduction of greenhouse gases earlier than planned in an attempt to secure the United States ' ratification of the protocol .####[([12, 28], [11], [4, 7], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA The U.S. backed out of the agreement , saying its industries would be handicapped by stringent rules that developing countries could simply ignore .####[([6, 7], [3, 4], [1, 2], 'Negative', 'Weak')]

NA If things go on like this , the government must transform the current industrial structure into an environment - friendly one and minimize industries which use a host of energy such as petrochemicals and cement manufacturing .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The government will have to pour a lot of money into businesses to promote energy efficiency .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA According to the United Nations ' climate panel , in the next 10 to 20 years changes in the climate will be almost unaffected by what we do in the way of initiatives in the next few years to reduce emissions of climate gases .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The explanation is that the increased concentration of climate gases in the atmosphere and the slowness of the climate system will make a certain degree of global warming unavoidable .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In recent years the RegClim research project , under the aegis of the Norwegian Research Council , has worked to estimate the way the climate will develop in Norway in 30 to 50 years .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The main conclusions were that the trend toward warmer weather and more precipitation will presumably continue .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The climate changes will be different from region to region .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA North Norway will also get more precipitation in the fall but warmer temperatures in the winter .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In the eastern part of Norway the biggest increase in precipitation will be in the winter .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In coming years the winters will be less snowy but greener and wetter .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA These extrapolations of the state of the climate are not completely reliable .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
