NA Space station 's railcar slightly off track####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA CAPE CANAVERAL - ( AP ) --####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Astronauts sent the international space station 's new railcar rolling slowly down a short stretch of track Monday , but it quickly hit a snag that interrupted the inaugural run of the first permanent railroad in orbit .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA NASA blamed the problem on weightlessness .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Engineers suspect the one- ton car floated ever so slightly off the rail , causing the magnetic sensors on the bottom of the car to lose contact with a pair of iron strips in the aluminum tracks .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The railcar will eventually be used during the next stages of the space station 's construction .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The track runs along a 44 - foot girder that space shuttle Atlantis ' astronauts delivered and bolted to the orbiting outpost last week .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The problem cropped up after the empty flatcar moved down 17 feet of track at a snail 's pace of less than a half - inch per second .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Right on cue , the car stopped at a work station and was automatically latching itself down when everything came to a halt .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Ground controllers took over manual control and , a few hours later , were able to latch the railcar to the track .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Space station astronaut Carl Walz sent another computer command from inside to get the railcar moving again .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The railcar smoothly rolled 26 feet to a second work station , where the same thing happened .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Again , ground controllers had to take over manual control to secure the car .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Later Monday , Walz commanded the railcar to move for the third and final time , back down the same 26 feet of track .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA '' The train 's leaving the station , '' he called out .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It got to where it was going , but the automatic latching system shut down again and ground controllers had to step in as before .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA '' I think what we 're finding out as we go through this is how the mobile transporter works in zero-g , '' said Ben Sellari , a NASA manager .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Engineers may adjust the computer software sometime if it becomes more of a nuisance , he said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA There is no danger of the $ 190 million railcar rolling off the track because of rings on both ends of the 44 - foot girder , Sellari said .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The first use of the railcar is set for late summer .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The railcar is needed to transport the space station 's 58 - foot robot arm from one end of the outpost to the other as more girders are installed .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]

NA In the summer of 1993 , the Marion County Commission on Youth began what can best be described as a " new era " in its history .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA MCCOY was reorganized as an independent , not-for- profit agency , separate from local government .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA It retained , however , the same mission with which it had been charged from its inception : to serve as a catalyst for effective , coordinated , and collaborative service delivery to youth in our community .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA For the past three years , MCCOY has been actively engaged in accomplishing this declared mission in cooperation with many others : youth service providers , youth , funding bodies , and interested citizens to name a few .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA We have met with a number of successes along the way , most notably the Summer Fun Line , the Metro Summer Bus Pass , and the development of ten neighborhood youth councils .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA A Providers Council and a Youth Coalition are building relationships that will hopefully bear great fruit in the years to come .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The formation of The Community Academy , a pilot project directed at expelled students from local school systems , has come about as a result of MCCOY 's efforts to mobilize community agencies in response to a pressing issue .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA McCoy is actively represented and working with numerous community collaborations where we regularly raise our voice to speak out for the inclusion of young people in both decision -making and program planning processes .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA One concrete example is a joint project undertaken in the United Northwest Area in partnership with The Junior League of Indianapolis and Community Partnerships with Youth from Fort Wayne , Indiana .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA As a team , these three organizations are working with neighborhood youth and adults to build a " Caring Neighborhood with Youth " , mobilizing the assets of young people and adults as partners to build a better neighborhood for all .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Since its re-organization , MCCOY has established its unique niche within the community by refraining from direct service programming and focusing on what it does best : helping to identify youth needs , convening groups of individuals and organizations which can address those needs , and moving toward collaborative solutions .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA McCoy has only one interest : the well being of Marion County 's young people .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA McCoy invites the support of The __ Company Foundation in the amount of $ 10,000.00 to support such activities as : ---- the co-ordination of youth leadership training and youth empowerment efforts at the neighborhood level by means of neighborhood - based youth councils ; ---- the promotion of youth employment opportunities ; ---- the facilitation of ongoing discussions regarding effective and efficient youth service delivery ; ---- the provision of technical assistance and guidance to neighborhoods which seek positive youth - adult relationships ; ---- the development of community - wide supports for the positive growth of all Marion County young people .####[([3, 15], [2], [1], 'Positive', 'Average'), ([80, 84], [79], [0], 'Positive', 'Weak')]

NA A Brief History Jerusalem ' s recorded history begins with its mention in Egyptian court records 4,000 years ago , but there had been human settlements here for centuries , probably millennia , before that .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA At the beginning of the second millennium b.c. , Jerusalem was a Canaanite mountain stronghold on a secondary trade route , far less important than biblical cities such as Hazor , Megiddo , Beth Shean , and Shechem .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The earliest name associated with the city , Ur usalim , perhaps meant ``city of Shalim ' ' or ``founded by Shalim .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA '' Scholars speculate that Shalim might have been an ancient Semitic deity of peace , for the name resembles the modern Hebrew and Arabic words for ``peace '' : shalom and salaam , respectively .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA If true , this is an ironic name for a city that would become one of the most constantly and bitterly embattled places on the face of the earth .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Biblical Jerusalem####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In the Bible , Genesis 14:18 -- 20 records that Abraham visited the city of ` `Salem ' ' in approximately 1800 b.c. and was blessed by the city ' s ruler , Melchzedik , who offered him bread and wine .####[([11], [25, 26], [28, 34], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA The city is not mentioned again in the Bible until the time of the great poet warrior , King David , who captured the city from the Jebusites in about 1000 b.c .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Bible describes how David ' s soldiers conquered Jerusalem by discovering a water tunnel under the walls and using it to take the city by surprise .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Warren ' s Shaft , part of a Canaanite water system discovered by 19th - century archaeologists and open to visitors , might be the very tunnel infiltrated by David ' s army .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Perhaps because Jerusalem was in neutral territory not allotted to any of the twelve rival tribes of Israel , David made it the capital of his newly formed kingdom and brought the most talented artisans , dedicated priests , magical poets and musicians , and the most formidable soldiers from each of the tribes to live in his city .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA He also brought the Ark of the Covenant , the portable tabernacle containing the Tablets of the Law received on Mount Sinai , to the Spring of Gihon , just outside the walls of Jerusalem .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA There the Ark rested until it was placed in the Temple , built in approximately 960 b.c. on Mt. Moriah , the high point at the northern end of the city .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Temple ( today known as the ` `First '' Temple ) was completed by David ' s son and successor , King Solomon .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA According to biblical tradition , although David bought the land for the Temple and carefully assembled its building materials , he was deemed unworthy of constructing the Temple because he was a man of war with blood on his hands .####[([21], [23], [3, 4], 'Neutral', 'Average'), ([0], [23], [3, 4], 'Neutral', 'Average')]
NA At the Temple ' s dedication , Solomon addressed his God : ``... the Heavens , even the Heaven of the Heavens , cannot contain####[([0], [9], [8], 'Neutral', 'Average'), ([0], [9], [8], 'Neutral', 'Average')]
NA Thee ; how much less this House that I have built ?####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ' '####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The site of the Temple eventually became identified as Mt. Moriah , on which it stood , where Abraham was called to sacrifice his son Isaac .####[([22, 26], [21], [0], 'Positive', 'Weak')]
NA Along with this splendid house of worship , Solomon built a royal palace , mansions for his wives , temples for the foreign gods worshipped by the princesses he had married , and towers for the defense of the capital .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Under the wise reign of Solomon , the city flourished as the capital of an empire that stretched from Damascus to the Red Sea and controlled the trade routes from Egypt to Phoenicia .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Temple and royal palace were adorned with gold and ivory from Africa and with cedar from Lebanon ; the beauties and glories of Jerusalem under Solomon have captivated readers of the Bible for almost 3,000 years .####[([20, 27], [29], [30, 33], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA But with his death the empire collapsed , and the Israelite kingdom was divided into two separate , impoverished , often warring nations : Israel , with its capital at Shechem in the north , ruled by a series of northern dynasties ; and the smaller kingdom of Judah , with its capital at Jerusalem , from which the Davidic dynasty continued to rule .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Bible tells us that the cruelty and impiety of the rulers of both kingdoms aroused the fury of the great Prophets .####[([11, 15], [3, 4], [1, 2], 'Neutral', 'Average'), ([6, 15], [18], [1, 2], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA In 701 b.c. the Assyrian armies of Sennacherib destroyed Israel and moved southward to besiege Jerusalem .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Thanks to King Hezekiah ' s hidden water tunnel , the city narrowly escaped destruction .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The end of David ' s dynasty came in 587 b.c. , when Nebuchadnezzar , King of Babylon , invaded Judah to lay siege to Jerusalem .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA When it fell , the Temple and all the buildings were burned .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The people of the once-glorious city were forced into an exile known as ``the Babylonian Captivity .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA ' '####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In time , the kingdom of Babylon was overthrown and the Israelites were permitted to return to Jerusalem in 539 b.c .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The city was now under the more tolerant rule of the Persians , but rebuilding was slow work .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Second Temple was finished in 515 b.c. , but much of the city still lay in ruins .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Jerusalem submitted peaceably to the rule of the Greeks in 332 b.c. under Alexander the Great and , subsequently , to his Hellenistic successors as well as the Egyptian Ptolomeys and the Syrian Seleucids .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA When Seleucid rulers outlawed Judaism , Jews led by Judah Maccabee and his brothers staged a revolution in 167 b.c. and , against all odds , restored the primacy of Jewish religious life in Jerusalem .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Macabbees cleansed the Temple of Hellenistic idols and the blood of pagan sacrifices ; the eight - day celebration of Hanukkah ( Feast of Dedication ) commemorates their victory .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Hasmonean dynasty , descendants of the Maccabee family , ruled an independent Jewish Commonwealth that stretched from the Negev to the Galilee .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Jerusalem grew , surrounded with a formidable wall and defended by towers beside the Jaffa Gate .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Hasmoneans ruled until Pompey ' s Roman legions arrived in 63 b.c. Roman Jerusalem####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA After the initial years of Roman administration and political infighting , Rome installed Herod ( scion of a family from Idumea , a Jewish kingdom in the desert ) as King of Judea .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA He reigned from 37 to 4 b.c. , during which time he fortified the Hasmonean wall and rebuilt the defense towers beside Jaffa Gate , the foundation of which still stand .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Several palaces were built and a water system installed .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Herod also completely rebuilt the Temple , making it one of the most important religious centers in the Roman Empire .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The courtyard around the Temple was expanded to accommodate hundreds of thousands of pilgrims , and the Temple Mount was shored up by retaining walls made with great stone blocks .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA One of these walls , the Western Wall , is today a major reminder of Jerusalem ' s greatness under Herod .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA A massive fortress was built overlooking the Temple Mount , which Herod named ` `Antonia ' ' in honor of his Roman friend and benefactor , Mark Antony .####[([21, 28], [13], [12], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA For all his accomplishments , Herod was nevertheless hated by his subjects ; he taxed , he tortured , and he ordered the massacre of male Jewish infants in an attempt to do away with the heralded Messiah .####[([6], [9], [11, 12], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA When Jesus was born in about 4 b.c. , Joseph and Mary escaped Herod ' s paranoia by fleeing into Egypt with the new-born infant .####[([0], [17], [14], 'Negative', 'Average')]
NA They returned to live in the Galilee village of Nazareth , making pilgrimages to Jerusalem .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA According to biblical accounts , Jesus spent his life ministering in the Galilee Valley .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In about a.d. 30 he and his followers went for Passover to Jerusalem , which was in unrest at this time , dissatisfied with Roman domination .####[([25, 26], [23], [13], 'Negative', 'Average')]
NA Jesus ' s entry into the Temple caused a commotion ; after the Passover dinner he was arrested by the temple priests , who were under direct Roman rule .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Jesus was put on trial quickly and condemned to crucifixion , a Roman form of execution for political and religious dissidents as well as for common criminals .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In a province rife with rebellion and retaliation , the execution in Jerusalem of yet another religious leader from the Galilee did not by itself have an immediate effect on history .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA After Jesus ' s crucifixion , harsh Roman rule continued until a.d. 66 , when the Jews rebelled .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA For four years Jewish zealots fought against the might of Rome .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA At the end , the Roman general Titus laid siege to Jerusalem in a.d. 70 , finally attacking its starved and weakened defenders .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Those who didn ' t escape were executed or sold into slavery .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Holy City and the Temple were destroyed .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The last of the zealots held out for another three years at Masada ( see page 76 ) .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Half a million civilians died in the Galilee and Judea as a result of this first revolt against Rome , a number unequaled in ancient warfare .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Christian and Islamic Jerusalem For 60 years Jerusalem lay in ruins , until the Roman Emperor Hadrian ordered the city rebuilt as a Roman town dedicated to Jupiter .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In outrage , the Jews began a second revolt against Rome , led by Simon bar Kochba .####[([0], [2], [4, 5], 'Negative', 'Strong')]
NA The ruins of Jerusalem were briefly liberated , but , in the end , Jewish resistance to Rome was defeated with great loss of life .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The planned new Roman city , Aelia Capitolina , was built over the ruins of Herodian Jerusalem , and Jews were barred from residing there for all time .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Jerusalem ' s physical existence as a spiritual city seemed finished , but its spiritual power for Jews , and for the struggling new Christian religion , remained .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA For the next two centuries Aelia Capitolina enjoyed an innocuous history .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But the Roman Empire became Christian in the fourth century , and Jerusalem became a center of religion once again .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Queen Helena , a devout Christian and the mother of Emperor Constantine the Great , made a pilgrimage to the Holy Land in 326 to identify the sites associated with Jesus ' s life .####[([0], [5], [1, 2], 'Positive', 'Strong')]
NA She found that the city ' s most beautiful Roman temple , dedicated to the goddess Aphrodite , stood on the site of the crucifixion .####[([10, 11], [2], [1], 'Neutral', 'Average')]
NA The temple was demolished and a vast , Classical - style church was built around Golgotha ( the hill where Jesus ' s crucifixion was believed to have taken place ) .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Throughout Jerusalem , other spots important to Jesus ' s life were commemorated with religious structures .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Pilgrims came from all over the Roman ( and , later , Byzantine ) Empire during the following centuries , but the prosperity they brought lasted only until 614 , when Persian armies overtook Judea and reduced Jerusalem to rubble again .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In 629 , Jerusalem was recaptured by the Byzantines .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Still reeling from the effects of the Persian devastation , Jerusalem was conquered in 638 by the forces of Islam .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Temple Mount was identified in Islamic tradition as ` `the farthest spot '' ( in Arabic , el-aksa ) , the site to which the Prophet Muhammad was transported in one night from Mecca on a winged horse , as described in the 17th chapter of the Koran .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA From here the Prophet ascended to the heavens and was permitted to glimpse paradise .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The rock on the Temple Mount from which he ascended , at or close to the site of the ruined Temple , was commemorated by the construction of the Dome of the Rock in 691 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Dome of the Rock remains Jerusalem ' s most striking monument ; it is counted among the most beautiful buildings ever created .####[([1, 5], [15, 16], [0], 'Neutral', 'Average')]
NA By about 715 , the El- Aksa Mosque , third holiest place of prayer in Islam ( after Mecca and Medina ) , had been built on the southern side of the Temple Mount .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Jerusalem continued under Islamic rule for the next four and a half centuries .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In 1099 , under their leaders Godfrey de Bouillon and Tancred , the Crusaders captured the Holy City for Christendom by slaughtering both Muslims and Jews .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Crusaders , Mamelukes , and Turks####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Crusaders established a feudal Christian state with Godfrey at its head .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA They built many impressive churches during the term of the first Latin Kingdom of Jerusalem , but in 1187 they were driven out by Muslim forces under the great warrior Saladin .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA During the Sixth Crusade ( 1228 -- 1229 ) , the Holy Roman Emperor Frederick II managed to secure Jerusalem for the Christians by negotiation .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Christians , however , could not hold the city .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA After they lost Jerusalem , a Mongol invasion swept through , and in 1244 the Mameluke dynasty of Egypt took control , ruling Jerusalem for the next 250 years .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The city struggled to rebuild from Crusader wars and invasions .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Much of the best Islamic architecture in the city was constructed in the Mameluke era , but the past thousand years had taken their toll : Jerusalem was unable to regain the prosperity it had enjoyed in earlier times .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In the early 16th century , the Ottoman Turkish Empire was advancing through the Middle East .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Jerusalem fell to the Ottomans in 1517 , remaining under their control for 400 years .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Suleiman the Magnificent rebuilt the walls and gates in the form they retain to this day .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Fountains , inns , religious schools , and barracks were constructed .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But when Suleiman died , his empire , including Jerusalem , began a long period of decline .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Holy City remained a backwater until the 19th century , when renewed interest among Christian pilgrims made it the destination of thousands of travelers each year .####[([1, 3], [13, 14], [16, 17], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA 19th -Century Aspirations####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA At the same time , many Jews sought religious freedom and fulfillment by moving to Palestine ( as the Holy Land was traditionally called ) and especially to Jerusalem .####[([9, 10], [8], [7], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA In the 1890s , Theodor Herzl ( 1860 -- 1904 ) worked to organize a movement , Zionism , to create a Jewish state .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Chaim Weizmann ( 1874 -- 1952 ) , a scientist born in Russia but later a British subject , did much to put Herzl ' s hopes into practice .####[([0], [27], [24], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA Weizmann was an important figure in the negotiations with the British government that led to the Balfour Declaration of 1917 , supporting the idea of a Jewish ``national home ' ' in Palestine that also respected the rights of existing non -Jewish people already living there .####[([23, 46], [22], [10, 12], 'Positive', 'Average'), ([37, 46], [36], [10, 12], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA The problem was that British strategists , who were fighting the Ottoman Turks in 1917 , had secretly promised the lands to their World War I Arab allies .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In 1922 the League of Nations granted the British a mandate to administer Palestine .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Jerusalem flourished during the early years of the Mandate .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Modern neighborhoods , hospitals , schools , and the Hebrew University were built in West Jerusalem , the new Jewish enclave .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But Arab opposition to new Jewish immigration and construction in Palestine led to increasing strife ; by 1946 , Jerusalem was an armed camp .####[([5, 11], [3], [2], 'Negative', 'Average')]
NA In 1947 the United Nations voted for the partition of Palestine into two states , one Jewish and one Arab , with Jerusalem as an international city that belonged to neither .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA But lacking the means to enforce its decision , the United Nations was powerless to halt the fighting that erupted as the British withdrew their troops in 1948 .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Modern Israel####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The State of Israel was declared during this difficult time .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA In response , member states of the Arab League sent troops to help the Palestinian Arabs .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA West Jerusalem , separated from the rest of the new Jewish nation , held out under siege for several months until Israeli forces secured a land corridor connecting the city to the coastal areas .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Jews were evacuated from the Old City ' s Jewish Quarter , and thousands of Arab families fled their homes in West Jerusalem .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA As a result of armistice agreements in 1949 , Jerusalem was divided : West Jerusalem was to be under Israeli control , and East Jerusalem ( including the Old City , with its Jewish , Muslim , Christian , and Armenian quarters ) came under Jordanian authority .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Free access to holy sites for members of all religions was guaranteed by the armistice agreements .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA However , with the city partitioned by fortifications and barbed wire , no Israeli or Jewish pilgrims were allowed to visit the Western Wall or other Jewish sites in East Jerusalem .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA For the next 19 years , Jerusalem was two cities .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Political and religious boundaries were aggravated by occasional incidents of terrorism or sniping until the Six Day War in June 1967 .####[([8, 13], [5, 6], [0], 'Negative', 'Average')]
NA Within three days the city was completely in Israeli hands , and in two weeks it was physically and administratively reunited .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Jerusalem ' s mayor , Teddy Kollek , spent the next 25 years orchestrating a vast program of development , adding new cultural institutions and parks and instituting neighborhood restoration projects while tirelessly me diating the concerns of Jerusalem ' s many communities .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Today , as always , Jerusalem is a city of controversies : religious Jews in conflict with secular Jews ; Palestinians calling for independence ; many residents protesting a wave of high- rise development that many claim will turn the Holy City into a holy megalopolis .####[([29, 34], [28], [26, 27], 'Negative', 'Average'), ([24], [22, 23], [21], 'Positive', 'Average'), ([18, 19], [15, 17], [13, 14], 'Negative', 'Average'), ([13, 14], [15, 17], [18, 19], 'Negative', 'Average')]

NA BETHANY - The number of illegal immigrants in Swaziland seems to be increasing .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA Last month members of the Umbutfo Swaziland Defence Force [ USDF ] found 594 illegal aliens in the country .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The USDF found 43 Somalians inside two kombis in Maphiveni and 23 others were found without travel documents at Matsamo border and were handed over to the Horo police .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA At least 507 illegal Mozambicans have been found , as well as eight South Africans , two Tanzanians , and one Burundian .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA According to the army spokesman , Corporal Nhlanhla Dlamini , the key areas where most of the immigrants were found was Lomahasha , Mhlumeni and Sitsatsaweni .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA " We have discovered that there is a certain family around Lomahasha , which is suspected of assisting illegal immigrants with shelter and transport .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The army would like to request whoever is engaged in this criminal activity , to stop , " he said .####[([7, 13], [3, 6], [19], 'Positive', 'Average'), ([7, 16], [3, 6], [19], 'Positive', 'Average')]
NA Last month , 53 cattle were also stolen around the country , of which 17 were spotted inside Mozambique driven by three men armed with rifles thought to be AK47s .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
NA The Mozambican soldiers have promised to act quickly .####[([0], [0], [0], 'NA', 'NA')]
